(Beiping) The Military Affairs Committee ordered that the Japanese infantry troops stationed in Beiping would hold drills on the 24th. At 5:00 AM, they passed through the Fadingmen gate and would return to Beiping on the 25th. Sixteen officers and soldiers were sent to Miyun and other locations. (Special dispatch, 24th)

Huang Fu to Return to Beiping Within Days 59

(Beiping) It is reported that Huang Fu will return to Beiping within days to handle various matters. After Song Ziwen returns to Nanjing from Japan, he will convene an important conference on financial and diplomatic matters before heading south to participate. (Special dispatch, 24th)

Commander of Volunteer Army, Tian Lin, Dies in Battle 60

(Beiping) Tian Lin, commander of the Volunteer Army, died in battle on July 27 in Nan Zamu, Qingyuan County. In that battle, more than 100 Japanese soldiers, leading more than 400 puppet troops, launched a fierce attack on our army under the cover of airplanes and artillery. The Volunteer Army advanced bravely, killing one Japanese captain, 13 Japanese soldiers, and more than 20 puppet troops. Tian was killed by enemy machine gun fire to the waist. His troops were collected and commanded by Zhao Bochao, Yu Baichuan, Gao Denghou, and Liu Zifu. The Volunteer Army unit of Jia Bingyi fought fiercely with the Japanese and puppet troops on the 15th of this month in the Qiongbangzi Diaoguan area east of Fangxin City. The enemy totaled more than 50 Japanese soldiers and one brigade of Yu Zhishan's puppet army, carrying dozens of machine guns and dozens of mountain and mortar guns. On the Volunteer Army side, Jia had gone to Beiping for medical treatment and was commanded by Li Zhuotian, deputy commander and commander of the Second Detachment, Yang Rongjiu, and engaged in fierce battles with the enemy. (Special dispatch, 24th)

Efforts to Shorten Travel Time for Beiping-Shanghai Train Service 61

(Beiping) The direct train service from Shanghai to Beiping will only be available when the Nanjing ferry service starts operating on October 10th. Starting from September 1st, the southbound train, originally taking 47 and a half hours, will be shortened to 40 hours and 45 minutes. The northbound train, originally taking 49 hours and 9 minutes, will be shortened to 43 hours and 48 minutes. The 20 new train cars purchased from England are all third-class cars. The 36-hour travel time between Shanghai and Beiping has not been implemented since 1924. Due to the condition of the tracks, it is not possible to travel at a faster speed, so it is not possible to restore the previous time. (Reuters telegram, 24th)

US Troops Stationed in Beiping Go to Tianjin for Rotation 62

(Beiping) More than 60 American soldiers stationed in Beiping, led by a military attache, went to Tianjin this morning for rotation. (Special dispatch, 24th)

Candidates for Tianjin Mayor Undecided 63

(Tianjin) Regarding the candidates for mayor, it is said that Huang Fu recommended two people, Wang Jingwei recommended one person, and Yu Xuezhong recommended one person. Wang is the most promising. (Special dispatch, 24th)

Tianjin to Establish More Free Schools 64

(Tianjin) There are too many out-of-school children in this city. The municipal government has decided to establish 46 more free schools, with an annual expenditure of 50,000 yuan. (Special dispatch, 24th)

He and Zhang Confer on Post-War Matters in Border Areas 65

(Hankou) He Chengjun and Zhang Qun conferred on the 24th on post-war matters in the border areas. He also summoned local gentry from Southern Hubei for instructions, urging them to return to their hometowns to assist in suppression of bandits. Cao Haosen went to Xun on the 24th to visit Chiang. Sun Lianzhong was ordered to concurrently serve as commander of the 42nd Army and returned to Eastern Hubei from Hankou on the 24th for defense. (Special dispatch, 24th)

[Handling of the Train Accident on the Nanchang-Xunyang Road]

(Nanchang) Regarding the aftermath of the train accident on the Nanchang-Xunyang Road, the railway bureau will issue compensation to the families of the deceased, cover medical expenses for the slightly injured, and provide long-term living expenses for the seriously injured. All derelict personnel are being detained for interrogation and will be punished accordingly. (Central News Agency telegram, 24th)

Mao Bangchu Talks About Zhang Xueliang's Donation of Aircraft as Untrue 68

(Hangzhou) Mao Bangchu, acting principal of the Aviation School, told reporters that the report that Zhang Xueliang purchased ten 210-horsepower aircraft in Italy and donated them to the Aviation School, which have already been test-flown in Hangzhou, is completely untrue. (Special dispatch, 24th)

Zhejiang Province Buys Land from the People for Road Construction 69

(Hangzhou) In recent years, Zhejiang Province has forcibly nationalized land along the routes of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and highways. The government originally claimed to provide compensation, but due to the lack of funds in the treasury, it has often failed to do so. The people still have to pay taxes on the land as before, and their hidden pain is difficult to express. It is now reported that the provincial government, in order to alleviate the people's difficulties, is urgently clearing up these land taxes. (Central News Agency telegram, 24th)

Hurricane Hits Eastern US 71

Unprecedented in 50 Years

Trees Uprooted, Houses Destroyed, Rivers Overflow

Salisbury Completely Destroyed, Washington Streets Flooded

Estimated Losses Reach Millions

Washington, National News Agency, 22nd – Washington and other towns on the Potomac River have experienced the worst storm in 50 years, uprooting trees and destroying houses, causing significant losses. The wind reached 80 miles per hour, and the rainfall reached 6.18 inches in 24 hours. The Potomac River overflowed in the lower reaches in Virginia, flooding several farms. One-third of Norfolk was submerged, accessible only by small boats, with losses exceeding $1.5 million. Virginia Beach and Ocean View, both famous summer resorts, also suffered losses of $1.5 million each, with looting occurring in both. The mayor has requested the government to send troops to assist the police in maintaining order, as the poor took boats to the homes of the wealthy, who had evacuated to higher ground, and looted furniture and clothing. There is still a low-pressure center nearby, and there is fear of more storms.

Washington, Reuters, 23rd – The hurricane that passed through the eastern coast of the United States yesterday has not yet subsided and has caused much damage, estimated to be in the millions of dollars. Norfolk, Virginia, alone suffered losses of no less than $2 million. The famous seaside resorts and the outskirts of Willoughby in that state have been destroyed by the storm. Streets in Washington are also flooded today. Many trees near the White House have been uprooted. The American ship Madison, carrying 37 passengers from New York to Norfolk, encountered the storm off Cape Charles. The ship's engines were damaged and unable to proceed. Two Coast Guard ships are protecting it. The cruiser Indianapolis has been ordered to sail out to assist when it receives the ship's distress signal.

Washington, Havas, 24th – Salisbury, Maryland, has been completely destroyed by the wind. The hurricane appears to have blown to Washington. Although the speed has decreased, many trees have been uprooted. Fallen trees have damaged cars and disrupted tram traffic. Airmail lines have been suspended. Naval stations along the coast and US warships have prepared to rescue ships in danger.

Managua, Reuters, 24th – Major earthquakes have struck Maragua and Nicaragua. Part of the city of Leon has also been destroyed.

Hitler Started as a Sailor 72

Helsinki, Reuters, Through Hill News Agency – A Finnish weekly magazine published an article written by a Finnish sailor, describing the situation of today’s world-renowned German Chancellor Hitler, who was an ordinary sailor on the British cargo ship Wolfe Clyde. It is said that Hitler worked diligently and had a talent for speaking.

Mussolini Handles the German-Austrian Problem 73

French Government Expresses Satisfaction

Paris, Reuters, 23rd – During the meeting between Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, the Italian Prime Minister stated that his only desire was to cooperate sincerely with France and England in handling the Austrian-German problem. As for the formation of an Italian-Austrian-Hungarian alliance, there is really no issue. The French government is very satisfied with the attitude of the Italian Prime Minister. The Italian and Austrian Prime Ministers also agreed to discuss and coordinate various aspects of saving Austria's economy with Austria, Hungary, Italy, Czechoslovakia, and perhaps other countries along the Danube River.

Vienna, National News Agency, 23rd – Austria's internal problems are now undergoing a rapid change, but its scope is still unpredictable. It is difficult to expect the current situation, which relies solely on emergency orders to maintain the situation, to last. It is predicted that before winter, Austria must have a new organization to save Austria's internal crisis. In this effort, there are already three distinct trends: The first is the establishment of a "strong government." Those who advocate this theory are Prince Starhemberg and Dr. Fey, and the Heimwehr organization is supporting them. The second faction is the Christian Social Party, centered on the current Prime Minister Dollfuss and Defense Minister Vaugoin. They strongly oppose the involvement of domestic troops in politics and are willing to organize a political committee to replace the old parliament without holding new elections. The third faction is led by the current Deputy Prime Minister Winkler, who is opposed to the first faction and is the mainstay of the pro-German faction. Their claim is that Austria is actually a part of Germany and should cooperate with the motherland.

Paris, National News Agency, 24th – Le Matin published a report from Rome saying that there are rumors in Italian political circles that the foreign ministers of France, England, and Germany will go to Rome in the second half of October to discuss everything with the Italian Prime Minister. Rome, Havas, 23rd – The Times published a news item from Vienna stating that Czech Foreign Minister Benes will come to Rome. Wheat Conference Sets Unified International Wheat Price 74

Standard Price Depends on the British Market

Advisory Committee Established to Temporarily Supervise Implementation

London, Reuters, 23rd – This afternoon, the International Wheat Conference, attended by representatives from 31 countries, has agreed on the international wheat price. This is a real step towards the international wheat agreement. It is reported that what has been set is the gold price for delivery at the destination dock, excluding tariffs. This price is based on the average market price of imported wheat sold weekly at British ports. The average market price of wheat will be maintained for four months, and then the importing countries can change their tariffs. This price will be discussed in French and American gold coins. The Wheat Advisory Committee currently being organized will be temporary in nature to monitor the implementation of the wheat agreement and to determine the measures contained in the agreement, but it will not monitor wheat production and trade. Major exporting countries and the Soviet Union will each have representatives to join the advisory committee, and the Danube countries will jointly send two representatives to join. The number of representatives sent by importing and exporting countries will be equal on both sides. It is expected that the final agreement can be obtained tomorrow.

US to Formulate Wheat Production Control Plan 75

Washington, National News Agency, 23rd – The US government has formulated a wheat control plan, mainly to greatly reduce the number of acres planted with wheat. Regarding exports and pricing, etc., will be changed at any time. Agriculture Secretary Wallace had originally planned to publish it tonight, but because he heard of progress at the London Wheat Conference, he temporarily postponed the disclosure. Wallace claimed that the United States is happy to join any suitable movement to raise wheat prices and regulate production.

US Authorities Work Hard to Promote Recovery Industry Regulations

Coal Industry Agreement to Take Time to Establish 76

Washington, Reuters, 24th – National Industrial Recovery Act Executive Officer General Johnson warned last night by broadcasting to those who obscured the axis and did not comply with the industrial recovery case, saying that they would find ways to force compliance with industry regulations. He further said that employers in the United States who agreed to increase wages and reduce working hours have accounted for one-third. Although President Roosevelt strongly urged industrial peace, there are still many labor disputes. The authorities implementing the recovery case have decided that although workers are free to choose their own labor unions, in the event of a dispute, an anonymous vote may be held, without adhering to the protests of the labor advisory committee. At present, the coal industry still does not have the prospect of establishing an agreement soon.

Washington, Reuters, 23rd – General Johnson, Executive Officer of the Industrial Recovery Act, discussed commercial lending with the Federal Reserve and the Financial Rehabilitation Corporation today to address the financial issues required by commerce in promoting the national prosperity plan. The methods to be adopted have not yet been agreed, but some progress has been made. General Johnson is still fully handling the coal industry issue. President Roosevelt has paid close attention to the complexity of this matter. The deadline for submitting the coal industry regulations will expire tonight, but the drafting of the coal industry and automobile industry regulations is proceeding very smoothly. The discussions on the retail industry have revealed a serious situation, because there are a large number of retailers in the country. If retailers are not subject to the provisions of the recovery regulations, it is feared that it will harm the business of large merchants.

Washington, Reuters, 23rd – General Johnson explained the collective bargaining clause in the Recovery Act, saying that the words "open shops or closed shops" cannot be included in current laws. Johnson's claim is to allow employees to work under the industry regulations organized in the public union or the labor union, but employers are not allowed to force employees to join the company's union.

Gandhi Wasting Away 77

The War Zone is Still Not Fully Recovered 80

Japan Refuses to Return Yuguan and Areas Outside the Great Wall

Bandits Run Rampant in the Xinglong Area, Our Police Force is Weak

Everything Will Be Negotiated With the Japanese Side After Huang Fu Returns to Beiping

Special Dispatch from Beiping: Of the counties in the war zone, only Yuguan City and the county areas protruding beyond the Great Wall have not been agreed to be returned by the Japanese side. After the recovery of Miyun County, the areas outside the city have also not been taken over due to rampant bandits. The War Zone Reception Committee, Yin Tong, Tao Shangming, Liu Shisun, etc., considering that Huang Fu and Yu Xuezhong are not in Beiping, should urgently discuss a concrete plan for all outstanding and pending matters to facilitate their implementation. Therefore, it was decided to hold a meeting in Beiping within the next few days to jointly determine the direction. As for the continuing banditry in the war zone, the security police are finding it difficult to quell due to their limited strength. There are currently no preparations for the establishment of an administrative inspector for the war zone; everything will be resolved when Huang Fu returns to Beiping.

Yin Tong, a member of the War Zone Reception Committee, issued a statement yesterday, roughly saying that the lost territories in the war zone have been mostly recovered and that the handover of Ping and Yu can be completely resolved. However, the reception of Yuguan has not yet been realized, leading to many misunderstandings in the outside world. In fact, since the death of Japanese Army Commander Muto Nobuyoshi, everything has come to a standstill. Therefore, all unresolved matters must wait for Hishikari Takashi to take office before negotiations can continue. In the future, the return of Yuguan should not encounter any difficulties. As for the import tariffs on goods entering from outside the Guan and the entry of vehicles from the puppet Fengshan Railway into the Guan for transportation, these can also be resolved after some negotiation. In short, there should be no further complications in the future. However, banditry is rampant in the territories of various counties, especially in Xinglong and Malanyu, where it is extremely rampant. The police force dispatched by our side this time consists of only over 2,000 officers, with each county being allocated only two to three hundred officers, which is a rather weak number. The Hebei Provincial Government originally planned to allocate 9,000 police officers in the war zone, but the number currently allocated is far from that. Tracing back to the deployment of police forces by our side after the recovery of the lost territories, the Japanese side did not fix any restrictions during the ceasefire agreement. If banditry is allowed to spread in these disaster-stricken areas, the future will be unimaginable. On this point, it is highly hoped that the Hebei Provincial Government will promptly organize the police force, strengthen its strength, and then actively implement the suppression of banditry to bring peace to the people as soon as possible. The various passes along the Great Wall line are still guarded by the Japanese army, and the issue of their return will also need future negotiations to be effective, but this will have to wait until Chairman Huang and Chairman Yu return before there is a suitable negotiation approach.

Zhao Enqing and over twenty other representatives of the people from the counties of the Dongji Beizhan area submitted a petition, because bandits are rampant everywhere. If special agencies are not established to thoroughly suppress them, it is feared that the police force is too weak, and the situation may spread, and the future will be unimaginable. Therefore, they came to Beiping to visit the military and political authorities and explain everything in detail. Yesterday, Zhao Enqing spoke about the rampant banditry in various places, saying that there are currently many bandits in the Luandongxi area, who kill and plunder at will, and it is deeply feared that this will cause diplomatic problems. Therefore, they have come to Beiping to petition the Military Branch of the Political Readjustment Committee, and the results are quite satisfactory. Currently, the bandit situation along the border can be divided into ten groups: 1) The Funing area, led by bandits Weng Lingge, Rong Shan, and Si Haijiao, has several thousand men, plus the small groups of Qingshan and Da Wulong, which are also no less than seven or eight hundred men. 2) Dongyangsheng has over seven hundred men, entrenched outside Liujiakou, while Xilaihao, Kouwailouzi, and Da Shire, with five to six hundred men, are also based near Liujiakou. 3) The bandit leader Lao Haozi and the Lingyuan bandit Zhang Dahuzi are both recruiting about a thousand men in the Doushan area of Qinhuangdao, with seven or eight cannons and over ten machine guns. 4) Si Haile has over four hundred men, based in the Qingshan area of Funing, with complete firearms. The number of people in Funing city who have fled to avoid bandits has increased to over 20,000. 5) The Tangdao River in Doushan County has a group of bandits of about two thousand men, with a considerable force. The bandit leader is Ma Wu, named Cheng Zhang, who is from Da Zhangzi outside the Guan and has over forty machine guns, sixteen heavy cannons, and over ten handheld machine guns. This group was originally a mutiny from a certain army, so they have plenty of weapons and ammunition. 6) Scattered small groups are located in Nan Shagou and Xiangshuilue in Lulong, Fenshan and Fenghuangshan in Changli, Changling in Luan County, and the Haixia area in Laoting, with dozens, hundreds, or hundreds of people forming gangs and becoming very powerful. 7) Over two hundred bandits were found in the North Langzhuang in Henghe Town, Lulong County, who indiscriminately rob and plunder. 8) There are thirteen bandit gangs in the Xinglong County area, with the bandit leader Zuo Shandiao having about three thousand men and running rampant in the Luowenyu area of Zunhua. 9) There are over four thousand bandits in the Jixian County area, causing the most damage. The bandit leaders are Wan Renchou and Si Haihong, etc. 10) There are over two thousand bandits near Xifengkou and Saheqiao. It is heard that the Japanese army brigade commander Hattori has telegraphed Li Jichun to Yu to discuss ways to suppress the bandits, and our side is paying close attention to this. (Jin)

The Water Level in Western Shandong Rises, Xuzhou Repairs Dikes to Prevent Disasters 81

The Water Level in Fengpei Drops, Already Out of Danger. The Provincial Government Dispatches Li Mingyang to Inspect Flood Prevention.

The Dike Repair Committee Builds a Ring-City Dike

Xuzhou Correspondence: The Xubu flood was fortunately averted, and the Fengpei flood has also been resolved. However, the water level in the upper reaches of western Shandong is rising daily, and the Xuzhou area is still not completely safe. Flood prevention work has not been relaxed at all, and post-disaster relief also needs to be addressed. Recently, the provincial government dispatched provincial committee member Li Mingyang to Xuzhou to inspect the water level and supervise flood prevention. The Dike Repair Committee is building a ring-city dike to prevent any eventuality. The situation of escaping danger and the recent situation of the water level are recorded as follows:

The Process of Fengpei Escaping Danger 82

The flooding of Fengpei by the Yellow River north of Xubu is due to the old river channel being higher than the terrain of Fengpei. The Dasha River, which connects the old channel and the Hui Lake, is a natural path for water drainage. Therefore, when the Yellow River headed north through the Dasha River on the morning of the 18th, it became torrential and unstoppable. The people of Fengpei initially wanted to build a dam on Gaozhai, but seeing that the Yellow River was irrigating the Dasha River, it had a high vantage point. The water was swift, and the river was narrow, causing head-on collisions. Dangerous lateral flows occurred at sharp bends. Huashan, Songlou, Baimiaokou, Fengji, etc., in Feng County, which are 12 miles away from the city, and Loulou, Youfangkou, Panlongji, etc., in Pei County, which are more than ten miles away from the city, are important junctions for the Dasha River to bypass the west side of Pei City and enter Zhaoyang Lake. The water flow was particularly rapid. Therefore, on the 18th and 19th, Feng City felt extremely dangerous, and Pei City was even more likely to be threatened. Fortunately, the water flow reached Zhaoyang Lake on the evening of the 19th, and the people of Fengpei were relieved. Zhaoyang Lake is connected to Weishan Lake and has always been a place for storing water. It is connected to Nanyang Lake in southern Shandong. Normally, the lake water is low and shallow, and the dry land on the shore is a great benefit to Pei County. The reason why the people of Fengpei previously dredged the Dasha River was to provide water for irrigation. They did not expect that the backflow of the Yellow River would cause harm. After the Yellow River entered Weishan Lake, it was stored, and the upstream source decreased. The old site of Dangshan has reported a drop in the water level, and the water overflowing the banks of the Dasha River has returned to the channel. However, the flooded fields have been completely submerged, and the disaster cannot be reversed. The county chiefs of Fengpei are trying their best to ensure the safety of the urban area and are particularly concerned about the recurrence of floods. Prevention has not stopped. Relief for the flooded rural areas has not yet begun, but the water in Weishan Lake has increased compared to before, and the lake fields have also been flooded. Fortunately, it has not yet overflowed the banks. If the water from western Shandong enters Weishan Lake again, Weishan Lake may also overflow, which is what the people of Fengpei are most worried about.

Investigation of the Water Level in the Upper Reaches 83

The source of the Yellow River in Xuzhou this time is all in the upper reaches of western Shandong. She Nianci investigated the downstream after flood prevention to prepare for further prevention. Mr. Tian initially arrived in Yanzhou via Jining, and then went to Jiaxiang from Jining. When he went to Juye from Jiaxiang on the 20th, he encountered the Yellow River on the way, and traffic was cut off. So he returned to Jiaxiang. He telegraphed She that the water in western Shandong was too high to trace back to Heze. He returned to Xuzhou on the 22nd. According to his report, the source of the Yellow River was all due to the breach of the river in Dongming, with a breach of more than fifty feet and a water depth of more than ten feet. The momentum was extremely fierce and rushed eastward, dividing into three streams. One stream in the northeast goes straight to Jining, and it will enter the canal. One stream in the east passes through Juye Jiaxiang and will rush to Weishan Lake. One stream in the southeast floods to Cao Dan, turning to enter Zhaoyang. The one in the northeast flows down the Zhao Wang River, the one in the east flows down the Zhu River, and the one in the southeast flows down the Wanfu River. Although the above rivers have river channels to follow, the water is too swift, and the river channels are narrow, overflowing everywhere and causing great harm. The Grand Canal connects to Weishan Lake. The Grand Canal passes between Jiangsu and Shandong, and Weishan Lake is the place for storage and drainage. Zhaoyang is connected to Weishan Lake. Although they are called two lakes, they are actually one. If all the water pours into Wei, northern Jiangsu will become a swamp. On the 21st and 22nd, Jia and Ju also received telegrams, Yuncheng was surrounded by the Yellow River, and the water outside the gates of Ju City was vast, and Jiaxiang was also feared to be unavoidable. Currently, all telegrams to the counties in western Shandong are forwarded by the Xuzhou Bureau to Guide and Cao County. The traffic to western Shandong is almost completely cut off, and the water is so vast that it has destroyed poles and damaged lines, and there is no way to repair them. The postal service has long been suspended, and the magnitude of the water can be imagined. As for how dangerous northern Jiangsu will be in the future, it is still unpredictable.

Preventing Downstream Floods 84

The only place that the Yellow River passed through in the west of Xubu is the old river channel between Fengpei and Xiaoai. The harm is only in the Yellow River. To the east of it are the old river channel of Pisuicui, and the Grand Canal. The old river has been silted for a long time, and the Grand Canal has also been abandoned for a long time. There is also the problem of transport water. Therefore, when the Yellow River came east, the authorities repeatedly telegraphed here to inquire. As the reporter said in his previous letter, after the Yellow River enters Wei, the disaster in the lower reaches will not be the Yellow River but the transport water. Now, the water in western Shandong will all take Weishan Lake as a teacher. If the water level of Wei rises, it will flow down along the transport, and Pisuicui will bear the brunt. After She Nianci sent a telegram to various counties to prevent floods, all counties have been prepared. Among them, Suqian County is the most disadvantaged, because the Yellow River Canal passes through Suqian City. Therefore, County Chief Feng once said that the Yellow River and the Canal came together, and the only thing to do was to wait for death. Moreover, the two rivers sandwiched the city, and the siltation has been for a long time. The bottom is high and the ground is low. Even if 200,000 people are recruited, they will not be able to block it. Fortunately, the water level has slowed down, and Feng has convened local flood prevention, and decided to rush to repair the Yellow River, the Canal, the Yang River, the Zao River, and the branch river dikes. There are city dikes, Si Cao dams, Yaowan dikes, Guanjiazhuang, Xu Taoyuan, etc. Each dike, and the various culverts of Chengxiang, Zhang Yao, He Zhuang, and Xiwu, all ten districts of the county, mobilized 26,000 workers to rush to repair them day and night. Pi reported that the water level had not risen greatly. However, according to the people in western Shandong and near the lake, according to previous experience, the water in western Shandong must flow through Wei for ten days before reaching it. Then the water from the three streams in western Shandong will have to wait several days before reaching Wei. After entering Wei, depending on the size of the water and the height of the water storage in Weishan Lake, it will be able to irrigate the Canal and flow downstream. The areas along the Canal can take advantage of this time to plan well and prevent things from happening.

The Provincial Government Dispatches Personnel to Prevent Floods 85

The provincial government attaches great importance to the floods in northern Jiangsu. Since Li Mingyang, a member of the Provincial Committee, is from Xuzhou, he was specially dispatched to Xuzhou to inspect flood prevention. Li arrived in Xuzhou on the morning of the 22nd by train from Pingpu. Accompanying him were item engineers from the Construction Department and Sangke members from the Security Department. After getting off the train, he stayed at the Garden Hotel. At that time, he accompanied She Nianci, the administrative commissioner of the twelfth district, and Wang Shicai, the director of the Public Security Bureau, in a car to Fengpei to inspect. He set off at 9:00 a.m. Before leaving, Li told reporters that the Yellow River in western Shandong had breached its banks and flooded northern Jiangsu. The reports from various counties were very serious. Therefore, the provincial government sent me to conduct on-the-spot inspections. This trip will go to Pei to inspect the water level of the Dasha River, then to Weishan Lake to inspect, and then to Feng County to inspect. After the Fengpei survey is completed, we will wait for the Yellow River to be surveyed in the old Yellow River channel in Gaozhai, Dangshan, and the water levels of Xiaoxian County. After the survey of the counties is completed, we will follow the downstream to survey the counties of Su, Pi, and Cui, focusing on flood control, and aiming to prevent or reduce floods in northern Jiangsu. It is checked that Mr. Li is familiar with the situation in Xuzhou, so he will be able to prevent everything. The people may be in danger of the fish. Commissioner She also reported to Li on the local flood prevention, rescue, and plans to completely repair the ring city dike, and requested the province to allocate funds. The Xuzhou group also plans to wait for Li to inspect and return to Xuzhou to meet with him and suggest that the provincial government allocate a large amount of water conservancy funds to repair the big dike, which will be a one-time solution.

Dike Repair Committee Meeting 86

Before the flood on the 15th, a committee was established to repair the Yellow River Dike. After the rescue, a meeting was held yesterday to decide to completely repair the ring city dike with all our strength, and block the road and Pipa Mountain dam to prevent the south irrigation of Weishan Lake, and replenish the dike of Wangzha Tianqimiao to resist the east encroachment of the west water. The army for rescue was given pig wine as a reward. After the dike is completed, we will continue to plan for the thorough dredging of the river in the territory. In the past, the counties were governed by themselves, and the interests of each other were conflicting. Now that the administrative area belongs to the twelfth district, we can plan comprehensively. I remember that in the 20th year of the Republic of China, the city of Xuzhou was flooded, and after the groups rescued and prevented the disaster, a commemorative stele of water disasters was published, pointing out the most details. The stele has also been published, and here is the inscription of the stele: "Xuzhou Water Disaster Precept Stele, in the summer of the 20th year of the Republic of China, the Xuzhou River was flooded and the embankment was broken. The residents were terrified. On August 7th, there was another heavy rain, and the water was three feet deep on the plain. The houses were floating. By dusk, it was suddenly reported that the embankment had broken in four or five places, and the water was about to enter the city. Everyone was shocked and ran away, not knowing where to go. Fortunately, officials and people rushed to block the embankment day and night, and it did not collapse completely. However, they were afraid that disaster was coming, and it has not ended yet. The Yellow River has been a disaster for Xuzhou for more than a thousand years. The dikes and defenses were the most solid. After the river moved, the officials and people loved and protected it without slackening. For the past eighty years, it has never been a disaster. This summer's rainfall is equal to that of ten years ago, and the danger is so great. The reason is that the local area has not paid attention to it for years, and there are few long-term plans. If it can be profitable in the present, it will open roads, build roads, flatten Guo, fill rivers, destroy dikes, and decide banks regardless. Therefore, some people use embankment stones to build roads, some people build tombs, some people take advantage of the opportunity to steal and sell them, and some people build houses along the banks. The embankment of thousands of years to protect the city and the stone bank built by millions of dollars will be destroyed in a few years. Internal and external blockages have almost caused a great disaster. Isn't it strange? The past is over, and the future can be pursued. However, at the beginning of the water retreat, people have not forgotten the disaster, or they still know the precepts. If they delay a few years, they will forget again. Those with foresight and long-term plans have also been vigilant and have considered this, but in the end, there is no remedy for the destroyers. The harm is gone, and people are easy to neglect. This association punishes the past and strives to maintain the status quo, and hopes to complete the embankment and dredge the river in the shortest possible time to eliminate water disasters and ensure eternal peace. If there is no regard for public hazards, arbitrarily blocking the river and deciding the embankment, it will be reported to the competent authorities for strict detention and punishment. Therefore, this stele is built to show the precepts. The gentleman of the country, please encourage each other." From this inscription, we can know the depth of the water disaster, but the dike defense is incomplete due to the lack of funds. How long has it been, and the water police reported again. This time, the meeting of the dike repair decided to complete the work of the great dike. I think the provincial government will have something to help with. (23rd)

The Shandong Relief Association Telegrams the National Government to Request Relief 87

The Disaster Area in Heze Accounts for Four-Ninths of the County

The Provincial Relief Association Asks for a Portion of the National Tax to be Used for Relief

Jinan Correspondence: Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Provincial Government and Chairman of the Provincial Relief Association, yesterday received a telegram from Wang Jiayan, County Chief of Yuncheng County, stating that the Yellow River has arrived in the county. It is also reported that Wang Shaochang, Deputy Dean of the Heze Rural Construction Institute, reported that the disaster in Heze was extremely severe, and the disaster area accounted for four-fifths of the county. Han believed that relief and assistance were the most urgent needs at present, so he telegraphed the National Government and the Executive Yuan again to request relief. The Provincial Relief Association also telegraphed the Central Government, requesting that, starting from the 22nd year, 10% of the national tax revenue in Shandong be retained for the purpose of saving the massive disaster. The various telegrams are recorded as follows:

Han sent a telegram to President Wang of the Executive Yuan, addressed to Executive Yuan President Wang Junjian, reporting repeatedly that the disaster situation in the counties of western Shandong was extremely severe, and asking urgently for prompt relief. I received your telegram stating that the Yuanhui decided that the Ministry of Finance should first transfer the unpaid amount of 600,000 yuan from the Yangzi River Flood Prevention Committee. Millions of lives in western Shandong are drifting and displaced, and their cries are everywhere. Relief cannot be delayed. I can only telegraph again and ask your Lordship to quickly order the Ministry of Finance to prepare the funds as soon as possible to save the survivors. I am grateful and awaiting orders. Sincerely, Han Fuqu bowed.

Han sent a telegram to Jiang, Wang, Lin, etc., addressed to Chairman Jiang of Guling, Executive Yuan President Wang, Chairman of the National Government Lin, Minister of Interior Huang, stating that the flood situation in the counties of western Shandong has been reported in detail. It is now based on the telegram from Wang Jiayan, County Chief of Cheng County, that the Yellow River arrived at the border at noon and flowed east in two streams, with the shallowest being two feet deep and the deepest being more than one zhang deep, and the current was turbulent. Also, according to Wang Shaochang, Deputy Dean of the Rural Construction Research Institute, the current flood disaster is extremely severe, and the area flooded in Heze accounts for four-fifths of the county, with more than a thousand villages completely submerged, and about 300,000 people affected, living in the open and lacking food, which is unbearable to witness. Please quickly telegraph the National Government to have mercy on the victims and provide generous relief. In addition to ordering the government to do its best to rescue them, I would like to report this telegram for your review and order relief to save the people. Sincerely, Han Fuqu bowed.

The telegram from the Provincial Relief Association to the National Government Executive Yuan Central Relief Association: Shandong Province has repeatedly reported the tragic situation to Han Fuqu, Chairman of Shandong Province and Chairman of this Association, and has asked for the rapid issuance of relief funds. It is checked that the river disaster came suddenly. Although this province has been able to prevent disasters by managing the river, other provinces have made the neighboring country a gully by breaching its banks. In addition, continuous yin rain and flooding have made dozens of counties and countless people into a swamp in a few days. Telegrams are requesting relief and awaiting orders. This association is in charge of relief and has an inescapable responsibility, but the relief funds have been suspended by the Ministry of Finance for a long time, and the requests have not been approved by the Central Government. Repeated calls have been ineffective. This association has no rice to cook, and the victims cannot be left to die. In addition to doing our best to plan and distribute emergency relief, all aspects of rescue, accommodation, prevention, and rehabilitation cannot be achieved without a large amount of relief funds. Please have compassion for the victims, quickly issue a large amount of funds, and also check the repeated telegrams from this association, and follow the provisions of the Premier's Outline of Nation Building to retain at least 10% of the national tax to handle local charities. Please allow 10% of the national tax revenue in Shandong to be retained for the rescue of the massive disaster, starting from the 22nd year, in order to help the people, which is extremely urgent. Shandong Provincial Relief Association Standing Committee members Li Shuchun, Zhao Xinru, Xin Zhujiu, Committee member Zhang Zicun, He Supu bowed. (23rd)

Military Tension in Northern Fujian Suppressing Bandits 88

Fierce Battles for Days, Over Five Thousand Red Bandits Killed or Wounded

Lu and Liu's Divisions Successively Recovered Mingxi and Tai Ning

Cai Tingkai Flew to Zhangzhou on the 15th to Command

The Counties in Northern Fujian Have Had Poor Harvests, and Refugees Are in Dire Need of Relief

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since being besieged by the Central Army, the Red Bandits in eastern Jiangxi retreated into northern Fujian and successively fell into Chong'an, Guangze, Taining, Jianning, Ninghua, Mingxi, Qingliu, Liancheng, and other counties. The situation in the upper reaches of the Minjiang River suddenly became tense. Later, the Liu Heding, Lu Xingbang, Zhou Zhiqun, Ma Hongxing, Nie Jinlong and other troops, guarded Jianyang, Shaowu, Jiangle, Shaxian, Yong'an, Pucheng, and other counties, and fought fiercely with the bandits. This went on for half a month. The Qu Shounian Division of the 19th Route Army also opened from Liancheng into Yong'an to coordinate defense, and the bandits began to fail. Among them, the Qu Division in the Liancheng area, the Lu Division in the Mingxi area, and the Liu Division in the Taining area had the fiercest battles. From August 1st to 10th, it is estimated that more than 5,000 bandits were killed or wounded. Our army also suffered considerable losses. Currently, Mingxi and Taining have been successively recovered by the Lu and Liu divisions, and the bandits have retreated to Qingliu and Jianning. The Qu Division has also advanced to the border of Liancheng for deployment.

Recently, the bandits changed their course to western Fujian due to repeated setbacks in northern Fujian. On the 13th, they attacked Longyan from Liancheng. In recent days, they have been in fierce battle with the Shen Guanghan and Zhang Yan divisions of the 19th Route Army. Cai Tingkai took off from the provincial capital on the 15th to fly to Zhangzhou to command, because the military situation in the front was urgent. The situation in northern Fujian has become more relaxed. However, since the beginning of this year, the counties in northern Fujian have suffered from drought and no rain, and the summer harvest has been hopeless. The areas producing rice in the Yanjanshao three counties used to transport Xi rice to the province for sale, but this year they have to come to the province to purchase sea rice and send it for relief. Now, at the time of the autumn harvest, they have suffered from banditry again. The farmers have fled to each other, and the fields have been left barren. Currently, tens of thousands of refugees in the bandit areas have fled to Jianyang, Shunchang, Jian'ou, and Jiangle. They are waiting to be fed. The county governments are unable to provide food and want to send them to the province. The Civil Affairs Department heard the news and urgently telegraphed to stop them, ordering them to set up shelters on the spot and allowing the province to allocate funds for relief. As for the refugees who have already arrived in the province, they were ordered to work with the various charities in Minhou County to find ways to provide relief. (August 17th)

Nanhui 89

The Songjiang Meat Ticket Was Cracked in Nanhui. Sun Fengchi, captain of the 4th team of the Datuan Aquatic Public Security Team, was ordered by the Minhang First District Team Department to assist Gong Fei, captain of the Songjiang County Aquatic Patrol, and Zhou Lianqing, captain of the 2nd team of the 1st team of the Songjiang Aquatic Public Security Team, to search the home of a Mr. Shen in Shenzhuang Beili Xu, 3rd District of this county for the Songjiang meat ticket. The Songjiang meat ticket Chen Xianjiang and Zheng Boxiang, and a bandit Shen Abing who was watching the ticket, were seized on the spot and sent to the Minhang First District Team Department for interrogation.

Suzhou 90

Further Arrests of Major Criminals in the Yancheng Kidnapping Case

Jiang Minsheng, a lake bandit who ran rampant in the north and south of the Yangtze River, was captured at the Tapiao Bin in Jiangwan, Shanghai a few days ago, and the Yancheng small meat ticket Wang Laixizi was rescued. He has been escorted to Suzhou and is being held in the Anti-Banditry Department's Investigation Team, pending interrogation. Captain Xu also discovered that Xue San, an accomplice of Jiang Minsheng, was hiding in the Zheng San Shipyard in Yangjing Town, Shanghai. He immediately led detectives Yu Lianyuan and others to Shanghai and arrested Xue San and Xue Wang at the destination. He is temporarily detained at the Second Branch of the Third District of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau and will be escorted to Suzhou for interrogation today (25th).

Gao Guiyou's Party Escorted to Suzhou 91

Gao Guiyou, the bandit leader of Taihu Lake, and the female bandit Wang Bamei, etc., were arrested by the Aquatic Public Security Team and escorted to the Suzhou-Song Aquatic Bandit Suppression Command. After interrogation by the military judge, they have been sentenced to death and submitted to the provincial government for approval before execution. Gu San Shao, a member of his party, was arrested by the First District of the Aquatic Public Security Bureau and escorted to the Bandit Suppression Command for interrogation yesterday (22nd) morning.

Appeal of the Changshu Murder Case Concluded 92

Last year, on July 20th, Yan Hongqing of the fourth district of Changshu, Shazhou City, and Jiang Qinsheng, who was a drill instructor in the local militia, caught his wife, Jiang Wang, having an affair with Yu Sanbao. The adulterous couple strangled Jiang Qinsheng to death on the 11th of the same month and buried his body in a mud pit in an attempt to cover up the crime. Later, Jiang Lisheng, the victim's brother, saw a pack of dogs digging at the mud pit and discovered the body. When he questioned his sister-in-law and nephew, Xiao Ying, they both claimed that Jiang Wang and Yu Sanbao had strangled Jiang Qinsheng. Jiang Lisheng reported the crime, and the Public Security Bureau arrested the adulterous couple, who confessed to the county government. The county sentenced both to death. They refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the Jiangsu High Court. Yesterday, Hu Shancheng, the judge of the Second Criminal Court, presided over the trial. Jiang Lisheng, the deceased's brother, and witnesses Gu Gaoer also appeared as summoned. The initial interrogation of Jiang Wang revealed that she was 38 years old. Her confession in Changshu was obtained under duress and was not factual. She denied being an accomplice. Yu Sanbao, 32 years old, also vehemently protested his innocence, denying any intimate relationship with Jiang Wang or involvement in the conspiracy to strangle Jiang Qinsheng. After the witnesses Gu Gaoer testified, Prosecutor Zhan Fen stood up and argued that the facts of the case had already been admitted by Jiang Wang and Yu Sanbao in the first trial and could not be denied. The death sentence was appropriate. After a lawyer presented a defense, the court declared the debate closed and scheduled the verdict for the 30th.

Wuxi

Female Worker Attempts Suicide, Moves Corpse to Frame 93

Tang Xiaomei, a 25-year-old unmarried female worker at the Gansheng Silk Factory under Gongyun Bridge, was of a fierce and impulsive nature. On the morning of the 21st of this month, she had an argument with Zhang, another female worker in the factory. Around noon the day before yesterday, Xiaomei gathered other female workers like A-cai and waited near the ferry crossing near the factory. When Zhang Qian arrived at the factory for work, they confronted her and violently beat her. Zhang Qian was pregnant and the assault caused her to be severely injured. Afterwards, her husband, Zhang Zhixiang, negotiated with Tang Xiaomei. Eventually, Xiaomei's brother, Ren Gen, apologized to Zhang on behalf of his sister, settling the matter. However, Tang Xiaomei was fired by the factory. Angered, Xiaomei committed suicide by drinking sedative water. Her family discovered her too late to save her. Her brother, Tang Ren Gen, believed that the incident stemmed from the argument with Zhang Qian. He blamed Zhang Qian and, yesterday morning (the 24th), hired workers to move the body to Zhang Qian's house at 9 Beicangmen. Zhang Qian was terrified upon seeing this and immediately reported the incident to Xi Xuechang, the head of the 13th Tu in that area, who reported it to the court for inspection. She plans to accuse the Tang family of moving the corpse to frame her.

Adulterous Couple Strangles Husband to Death 94

Gu Yunsheng, a 36-year-old villager from Shangtang Village, Wusan Tu, about three miles from Anzhen in the eighth district (Huai Township), lost his father early in life. His mother, Zhang, could not bear her widowhood and secretly became intimate with Ding Enrong, a local thug. Yunsheng discovered the affair and advised his mother kindly. Zhang felt that the affair was exposed, and it was a matter of face. She went to Suzhou to work as a maid. However, Ding Enrong hated Gu to the core. Gu's wife, Zhang, who was past her youth, also felt that her husband was not handsome and that there was a wide age gap between them. She also became intimate with Sun Awu (27 years old), a villager. They secretly met from time to time. On the 20th of last month, Gu came to the city to buy goods and returned home late at night. He saw a dark figure rushing out of the door. He questioned Zhang sternly, but Zhang made excuses. The next day, Zhang conspired with her lover, Ah Wu, and asked Enrong to help them kill Gu Yunsheng. Enrong hated Gu and was bribed with money from Ah Wu. He agreed to assist the adulterous couple in killing Gu. On the 30th, around 11:00 PM, Zhang took off her clothes and opened the door to let Sun Awu and Ding Enrong into the house while her husband was asleep. Zhang stuffed cotton into her husband's mouth, Ah Wu held down his legs, and Enrong used a hemp rope to strangle him to death. Afterwards, they tied a large stone to the body and threw it into the nearby river to cover up the crime. At 11:00 AM on the 23rd, a water-pumping boat turned on its machine and passed through the area. The body was dislodged and floated to the surface. The incident was reported to the 16th Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Chief Tan of the branch received the report and led police officers to investigate. He hired a net boat to retrieve the body. The entire body was naked and had not yet decomposed. There was a hemp rope tied around the waist, and there were marks on the neck from the strangulation. The adulterous woman, Gu Zhang, the adulterer, Sun Awu, and the accomplice, Ding Enrong, were all arrested and interrogated. They confessed to conspiring to kill Gu Yunsheng. The bureau chief believed it was a major murder case, so yesterday (the 24th), the three criminals were transferred to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation. After the case occurred, Tu Hezheng Pu Zhongying reported it to the county court, requesting an inspection.

Nantong

Police Detective Falsely Accuses Bandit, Transfers to Court 95

Wang Xiaoan, a police detective from the Taicang County Public Security Bureau, falsely accused Yu Junhai of being a bandit from Taicang because of a dispute over his mistress, He Guixiang. The county bureau, because Wang Xiaoan had no official documents and the case was already clear, transferred Yu and Wang to the county government. County Magistrate Ye summoned He Guixiang to court to testify. He then transferred all the witnesses to the court.

Dredging the Lower Reaches of the Yangtze River 96

The riverbank of Nantong collapsed greatly. The Yangtze River Waterway Management Committee advocated that local capabilities should be used first to maintain the twelve embankments that have not collapsed, so that the collapsed shoreline would not be prolonged and expanded. Since the lower reaches of the Yangtze River are a whole problem, the central government decided that engineers from the United States and America would draw up a plan to protect the areas that have collapsed below Jiangyin and develop the areas that have risen to fix a water channel for the Yangtze River. The construction cost is estimated to be 3.5 million yuan.

Mediation Attempted in Incense Industry Dispute 97

Liu Zhenxian, the executive director of the Incense Industry Union, previously reported that employers in the city, such as Yu Detai, had reduced daily wages by 6.2 cents, causing resentment among the workers. Although discussions were held, no results were obtained. The union then petitioned the party and government organs for mediation. It is heard that the county party headquarters, to understand the situation of both parties, recently summoned labor and capital to separate talks. Both parties sent representatives to state their cases. After these talks, the department will hold the first labor-capital mediation meeting in the coming days to avoid disputes.

Two Bandits Sentenced to Imprisonment 98

The Jiangdu Branch of the Zhenjiang Court previously found two bandits, Wang Jinlong and Jin Yongkang, from the Feilong Motor Transport in Zhenjiang. They were questioned in custody. Yesterday, the interrogation was concluded and Jin Yongkang was sentenced to twelve years in prison, and Wang Jinlong was sentenced to six years in prison.

Xiaoshan

Hurricane Capsizes Boats, Drowning Many 99

On the 22nd, at noon, in the Dingxiao River of Xiaoshan, a thunderstorm and hurricane occurred. Two cargo boats sailing from Linpu to Shaoxing were capsized by the wind. All the goods sank to the bottom of the river. Three boatmen and passengers drowned. At the same time, three small rowing boats, which were Shaoxing rice shop collection boats, with six bill collectors on board, were also overturned by the hurricane, and four people drowned. In addition, a fast boat from Xixing to Shaoxing overturned when it sailed to Yangfan Bridge, drowning two male and female passengers.

Yuyao

Opening of the China Land Reclamation Bank Office 100

The China Land Reclamation Bank has set up an office in Yuguan Street, Yuyao, to circulate funds in the interior and help rural revitalization. It opened today (the 24th). Qin Runqing, chairman and general manager of the bank, and Yu Zuochen, manager of the Ningbo branch, personally came to Yao to preside over the opening ceremony. Congratulatory messages from all walks of life poured in. Yuyao is the main cotton producing area in eastern Zhejiang. The annual output is worth 10 million silver yuan. The Zihai area is especially rich in salt benefits, and the straw hat cords woven by women are also a major export product of eastern Zhejiang. In recent years, the domestic financial situation has been stagnant and the market has been depressed. The bank is extremely willing to do its best to help the revival of the rural economy.

Hangzhou

Execution by Firing Squad of Murdering Arsonist 102

The Zhejiang Provincial Security Department determined that the Red Bandit Ren Boxiang (aka Ren Changxun) was originally engaged in kidnapping and killing in Yongkang and committed numerous crimes. In November of the 19th year of the Republic [1930], he surrendered to seek self-renewal, which was approved by the county and reported to the provincial government. In October of last year, Ren relapsed and, together with Ying Zhiying and A-ming from Taimen, resumed activities. They carried firearms to Xianju to collude with the bandit leader "Quezui Hong". When they returned to Yongkang and passed through Cao Dian in Xianju, they attempted robbery. The local militia caught them on the spot and shot Ying A-ming and Feng Mingdai to death, seizing one wooden-cased gun. Cao Dawang, a member of the militia, was injured and killed by the bandits. The case was sent to the Fifth Regiment and then to the Provincial Security Department. Interrogation revealed that the criminal joined the Red Army, committed murder and arson, and continued to collude with traitors and endanger the Republic and disrupt public order after his self-renewal. The evidence was conclusive and he was sentenced to death. Yesterday (the 24th) at 9:00 AM, he was taken to the execution ground outside Qingbo Gate and executed by firing squad.

City News

Tang Youren's Remarks After Arriving in Shanghai 104

Denies Government's Change in Diplomatic Policy

Envoy Jiang Zuobin Will Not Return for Time Being

Finance Minister Song May Have Social Engagements in Japan; No Telegram Received

Tang Youren, the newly appointed Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, accompanied by Madame Chen Bijun, the wife of President Wang, and Minister of Railways Zeng Zhongming, on the overnight train from Nanjing. At 10:00 AM yesterday morning, Mr. Tang met with reporters from various newspapers at his residence and firmly denied the rumors that the Central Government's diplomatic policy had changed. He also stated that Envoy Jiang Zuobin would not be returning to his post for the time being. Mr. Tang, along with Zeng Zhongming, Yu Youren, Zhang Zhijiang, and others, took the overnight train to Nanjing last night. Mr. Tang's remarks are summarized as follows:

Diplomatic Policy Unchanged 105

Rumors have been circulating in Nanjing and Shanghai in recent days that the Central Government's diplomatic policy has undergone some changes. Mr. Tang firmly denied these rumors. According to Mr. Tang, Minister Luo is scheduled to depart for Singapore tomorrow (the 25th). During Minister Luo's absence, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will be temporarily headed by President Wang concurrently. However, the Central Government's foreign policy remains the same and will not change. As for my visit to the Japanese Ambassador to China, Akira Ariyoshi, a few days ago, it was purely a matter of personal courtesy and did not involve any specific mission. The Japanese Ambassador had previously visited Nanjing, so I took the opportunity to return to Shanghai last week and paid a return visit to Ambassador Ariyoshi.

Envoy Jiang Will Not Return for Time Being 106

Regarding the question of the return of Envoy Jiang Zuobin to Japan, some people at the Lushan Conference asked Mr. Jiang to return to his post as soon as possible. However, Mr. Jiang himself is unwilling to return for the time being. Therefore, the rumors that Mr. Jiang would return to Shanghai from Lushan and travel east in early September are not true.

Finance Minister Song's Visit to Japan 107

Finance Minister Song Ziwen is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 29th aboard the President Jefferson of the Dollar Steamship Lines. A Reuters dispatch stated that Mr. Song, led by Zhang Gongquan, General Manager of the Bank of China, will visit various figures in Japanese political and business circles while returning to China. This is not the case. The Central Government has not received any telegram from Mr. Song stating that he will visit Japanese authorities. However, in accordance with international protocol, it is possible that he may attend social engagements ashore.

Use of US Wheat Loan 108

The use of the US wheat loan should be carefully studied. Regarding the Reuters dispatch stating that the US side expressed dissatisfaction that the Chinese government would use this loan to order machinery from the UK and Germany, Mr. Tang stated that he found this incomprehensible. Although the Central Government has not yet decided on the use of this loan for construction purposes, it still needs to be discussed in detail after Finance Minister Song returns to China.

Liu's Appointment to Europe Confirmed 109

The reporter then inquired whether the rumor of the former Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Liu Chongjie being appointed as envoy was true. Mr. Tang replied that the rumor that Mr. Liu would be sent abroad was indeed true. However, whether he would be appointed as envoy has not yet been determined, as the appointment of foreign envoys requires the prior consent of the host country. What I can tell you is that Mr. Liu has been confirmed to be appointed to Europe. As for which country, it will be officially announced after the consent of the host country has been obtained.

Shanghai County Party Headquarters Cables Opposition to Continued Winter Grain Tax 118

Demands Unified Stance

According to Daily News, the Shanghai County Party Headquarters has expressed strong opposition to the Jiangsu Provincial Government's recent request to the central government to continue levying an additional two yuan per picul of winter grain tax this year. It has also telegraphed all county party headquarters and agencies in the province, demanding a unified stance and joint efforts to fight for the interests of the people of Jiangsu. The original telegram is transcribed below: To all county party headquarters, directly affiliated district party headquarters, county public fund and property management offices, county food management committees, and county chambers of commerce in Jiangsu Province: It is well known that the land tax in our province is the highest in the country. In recent years, the amount of various taxes levied on each county's fields has already exceeded several times the regular tax. Although the name of labor tax has been abolished and changed to land value tax, it has in fact exceeded the late Premier Sun's legacy of one percent taxation on every hundred yuan in value. Moreover, in recent years, the rural economy has continued to decline, and the farmers' livelihoods have become more difficult. Land value has decreased rather than increased, and the government is seeking relief. However, it was recently heard that the Jiangsu Provincial Government has again requested the central government to continue levying an additional two yuan per picul of winter grain tax this year. Upon hearing this, we were greatly surprised. This additional levy originated during the Sun Chuanfang era and was called "borrowed grain tax". At that time, there was a clear statement that it would be deducted in the following year. In the 17th year [1928], it was continued for one year and renamed "Northern Expedition Donation". In the 18th year [1929], it was originally discontinued. In the 19th year [1930], the provincial government used the pretext of provincial treasury shortages to request and approve its continuation for one year. The glorious laws clearly stated that it would only be collected for one year and would not be extended. Unexpectedly, year after year, the government repeatedly broke its promises to the people. Speaking of this, we cannot help but feel disappointed. Now, low grain prices are hurting farmers, and farmers' income is barely enough to survive. As a result, they are abandoning farmland and flocking to the cities. The countryside has become bankrupt. Our central government is organizing a Rural Reconstruction Commission to plan for relief. Local governments should reduce taxes and levies to alleviate the people's plight. How can they act perversely, imposing extra taxes outside the law? The county party headquarters feels that the situation is critical and cannot remain silent. Therefore, it is submitting this document to your organization for review and verification. In accordance with our party's commitment to protecting farmers, we urge you to promptly forward this to the central government and the National Government, ordering the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance to strictly reject the Jiangsu Provincial Government's request to continue levying additional grain tax in order to alleviate the farmers' hardships and prevent rural bankruptcy. This is the duty of the Party. I hereby send this telegram, hoping that you will unite in advocacy and struggle to protect the people of Jiangsu and alleviate the hardships of farmers. Ma, Executive Committee of the Kuomintang Jiangsu Provincial Committee, Shanghai County.

Yao Wen-nan's Two Submissions 119

Shanghai gentleman Yao Wen-nan submitted a petition to the Municipal Government regarding land value tax and housing rental rules, stating his concerns. The following is a record of the submissions:

Submission One: A Petition Regarding the Implementation of Land Value Tax in This City, Which Property Owners Cannot Afford, Humbly Requesting Approval for Delayed Implementation to Alleviate the People's Hardships and Align with Public Sentiment. It has recently been reported multiple times that your government has announced the "Provisional Land Value Tax Regulations for This City," along with detailed implementation rules and organizational regulations for the valuation committee. The tax rate is set at six per thousand, and the tax collection date is set to begin on August 1st of this year. Upon hearing this, property owners have expressed their dismay. They believe that land consolidation is a policy of unifying tax revenue initiated by the late Premier Sun Yat-sen. The central government will have comprehensive plans for this policy in the future and should have a holistic approach. Currently, the Land Law has not been implemented. The central government also considers this matter significant and emphasizes caution, so it has not yet issued a unified national tax rate. However, this city is urgently announcing this separate law, setting a national precedent, which is unfair to the people's burden. Moreover, in civilized countries, any increase in the people's burden must be approved by a representative body of public opinion before it can be implemented. The Provisional Municipal Assembly of this city has already been established. Although many assembly members are from other provinces, they are all respected figures of the time and have the qualifications to represent the people. Although this land value tax measure has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval by your government, it has not been decided by the representative assembly of public opinion, and there is no obligation to bear the burden according to the law. Furthermore, since Shanghai experienced the war of January 28th, it has not yet recovered. It is hoping for time to recuperate and rebuild, and there is no surplus capacity to increase the burden. Upon investigation, the tax rate for the land value tax collection is much higher than the original land tax. The amount has increased several times in small cases, and tens or hundreds of times in large cases. After the people have experienced great trauma, the sudden direct increase of such a burden is beyond the capacity of the people. Even in terms of the currently promulgated land value tax collection measures, the land price is determined by the property owner. This was seen in the late Premier Sun Yat-sen's instructions. However, upon examining the detailed rules for the implementation of the provisional land value tax collection regulations, although the property owner also reports, the land price is actually determined arbitrarily by the valuation committee. Moreover, the members of the committee are all section chiefs from your government and its subordinate bureaus. Citizens have no right to participate in representation. With such measures, the prices determined in the future may not be fair. If the price is not fair and citizens are hastily required to fulfill their tax obligations, who will be willing? Isn't it only right to investigate whether tax collection is fair? This is an easy principle in economics. In 1929, your government announced the conversion of the general tax into a housing tax, collected equally from landlords and tenants. At that time, it was repeatedly stated that this was a transitional measure before the promulgation of the land tax. In the future, after the land tax law is promulgated, the landlord will bear the land tax, and the tenant will bear the housing tax. This is not only seen in the instructions of the former Director of the Finance Bureau, but also specified in Article 4 of the Housing Tax Collection Regulations of this city. Now, the land value tax has been scheduled to start collection, but how the housing tax collection method will be changed has not been announced at the same time. Property owners are very suspicious, and the autumn housing tax has already started to be collected. However, the method of equal sharing between landlord and tenant remains the same. The special levy has lost the credibility of the citizens and has placed a double burden on our property owners, which is unfair to the principle of equal taxation. All of these are things that our citizens cannot accept. I have always admired the mayor for his compassion for the people's hardships and his attention to detail. We believe that the time for this land value tax has not yet arrived. Therefore, we have jointly stated the reasons and submitted a written request to your government for review and approval to delay the implementation to alleviate the people's hardships and align with public sentiment. We are extremely anxious to await your orders. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Government.

Submission Two: A Petition Regarding the Promulgation of Housing Rental Rules in This City, Which Are Difficult to Implement, Humbly Requesting Approval for Repeal to Avoid Disputes. It has recently been reported that your government has promulgated seventeen articles of the "Housing Rental Rules for This City," which have been scheduled to take effect on August 1st. Upon hearing this, citizens have expressed their doubts and suspicions. It is generally believed that the promulgation of these rules is due to the difficulty in resolving rental disputes in this city, so this measure is specially set up to provide relief. It is the authorities' great intention to protect the rights of our property owners. If it is beneficial to promote in terms of law and fact, our property owners will all offer incense and prayers. However, upon reviewing the content, the entire judiciary is suspected of being fragmented. For example, guarantee of debt, termination of real estate lease contracts, etc., the civil law promulgated by the central government has clearly stipulated that it is purely within the scope of the judiciary and absolutely cannot be encroached upon by administrative authority. Moreover, upon investigating the guarantee responsibility stipulated in the rules, it is limited to two months' rent. If the landlord declares termination of the contract and orders the tenant to move out, three months' notice must be given in advance, and various restrictions such as exemption from two or three months' rent must be given. This means that the rental conditions and period completely lose the freedom of contract and clearly contradict the spirit of the current civil law. Even regarding the crackdown on rent arrears, according to the original Rule 4, if the tenant owes rent for three months, it should be handled according to Rule 13. However, Rule 13 states that if the tenant owes rent for more than three months, the police district should be reported to handle it according to these rules. However, after reviewing the entire text of the rules, there are no regulations on any method. Such vague wording is somewhat ridiculous. As a result, there is still no effective solution to rental disputes, and our property owners are at a loss. This is difficult to implement in terms of law and fact. Furthermore, upon investigation, the rent book stipulated in Rule 2 is stipulated to be purchased by the landlord from the police district in charge. However, now the police station in each district has sent police to sell this rent book to each tenant, and the price is deducted from the rent. Such a method is too disturbing and should be strictly prohibited. I have always admired Mayor Lu for his open-mindedness and willingness to accept good advice. Therefore, we have jointly stated the reasons and submitted a written request to your government to review and approve the repeal of the Housing Rental Rules to avoid disputes and align with public sentiment. We are extremely anxious to await your orders. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Government.

Continued Report on Restrictions on Chinese Immigration to Singapore 123

Singapore has the largest number of overseas Chinese, and many businesses are operated by overseas Chinese. This year, rubber and other items in the area have been affected by the global economic downturn. The number of factories reducing workers and suspending production is increasing day by day, and the number of unemployed workers in the area is increasing day by day, so there is a restriction on Chinese immigrants. This matter has been recorded in this newspaper. Now, after detailed investigation by reporters, the situation is recorded as follows:

Quota Regulations: Since the end of last month, when European postal ships traveling from Shanghai to Europe carrying overseas Chinese to Singapore encountered the problem of being prohibited from landing upon arrival, the European class of wheel companies, for business reasons, reduced the sale of tickets to Singapore, while consulting the British Consul in Shanghai, whether there are any restrictions on the number of overseas Chinese going to Singapore in the future. At the same time, they wired the Singapore branch to inquire with the colonial government to avoid disputes. Telegrams went back and forth and were discussed for a long time. It is now heard that the colonial government has agreed that each postal ship from Shanghai to Singapore shall carry no more than 25 Chinese passengers. If the quota is exceeded, a fine of no more than 1,000 Singapore dollars will be imposed for each Chinese passenger.

Ticket Purchase Restrictions: The Singapore colonial authorities, under strict restrictions on the number of Chinese going to the Nanyang Islands, and those going to Singapore, those of property class and substantial merchants, and those who travel, because they go to Singapore, belong to the surplus of life, and are prepared to go to consumption, or are related to trade, and are also sufficient to make Sing埠 profit, there is no problem at the time of entry, and it is still convenient to purchase tickets and sign for a passport. If there are no wealthy Chinese who want to go to Nanyang to seek a living, it is very difficult at the time of entry, and it is not easy to purchase tickets and sign for a passport.

Strict Inspection of Private Stowaways: Often, ship personnel of cargo ships privately accept bribes and hide laborers on board at Chinese ports, or hide them in cargo holds or pose as sailors, and secretly bring them to the new ocean islands to sneak into the country. It has been discovered many times. Therefore, the colonial authorities have strictly inspected cargo ships from Chinese ports to Singapore and other ports to prevent the smuggling of Chinese into the country.
