Members of the Postal Affairs Associations Issue Responsible Remarks 126

Regarding Post Office Layoffs

The postal authorities, in order to compensate for the current postal losses, have decided to forcibly retire more than 30 senior personnel across the country starting on September 1st of this year. This matter has aroused strong opposition from the postal affairs associations. According to a certain standing committee member of the postal affairs associations, he issued responsible remarks yesterday, saying: "The biggest reason for the post office's economic losses is due to the separation of the savings and remittance bureau, the subsidies for airlines, and the unrestricted transfer of funds from the Ministry of Transportation. In view of the seriousness of the situation, if this continues, the postal economy will be on the verge of bankruptcy. In the past year, we have thoroughly reviewed the reasons for the post office's economic losses, drafted a plan to consolidate the postal base, and adopted strike measures to seek implementation. The government representative and local leaders accepted the principles, and in May of this year, the Postal Economic System Research Committee drafted an implementation outline and recommended that the authorities adopt and implement it. However, to this day, the savings and remittance bureau is still separated, and the airline subsidies have reached more than 300,000 yuan in the past six months. As for the transfer of funds to the ministry, it was originally 30,000 yuan per month. After the separation of the savings and remittance bureau, it increased by 30,000 yuan per month. After the postal protection movement last year, it increased by another 30,000 yuan per month. If we think about it, how can the postal economic situation not get worse under such a situation? Under this situation, the postal authorities suddenly abandoned the fundamental and pursued the superficial, forcibly retiring a part of the personnel, and changing the pension fund subsidy from 7% of the total salary of the national employees to 5%. Upon investigation, postal employees enter the bureau after passing the examination, and their positions are guaranteed. There is no precedent for forced retirement. According to the Postal General Administration's training order No. 26768803, these members have served for a long time, are relatively old and weak, and their work is mediocre and their performance is poor. However, the ages of the laid-off personnel are all around 52 or 53, and according to regulations, they can serve until they are 60 years old. They are not old, their bodies are quite strong, their strength has not declined, and they are all important positions, and there is no failure to know. The report of the result is not mediocre, and the performance reports are excellent. The so-called bad news will be attacked. The authorities forcibly laid off personnel with unwarranted accidents, and the employees' positions have no security. The people are in a state of self-danger, and the postal efficiency will be greatly affected. In addition, the pension system is excellent and good. Postal employees are so loyal and diligent because they will have funds to support themselves after retirement and are not worried about leaving the country. Now the postal authorities have reduced the subsidy by 2%. If this is done, the pension will inevitably be shaken, people will panic, and the postal system will be disrupted. For the sake of protecting the post office, this association has always sought a thorough solution and has consulted with the ministry to seek a proper solution. The ministry has expressed that it is very calm. Unexpectedly, Huang Naishu, Director of the Postal Bureau, insisted on his own way and obstructed it. I don't know what his intention is. If he wants to destroy the postal system and cut the benefits of employees, this association will do its best to deal with it."

Ministry of Transportation Implements Radio Control 128

All Radio Stations are Registered and Calibrated

Planning to Implement Broadcasting Inspection Recently

In this city, there are more commercial radio stations than government-run ones, and many of them are not controlled by the Ministry of Transportation. Even among the radio stations, they do not communicate with each other, so there are often confusions and conflicts between the sound waves of the two radio stations. In view of this, the Ministry of Transportation is implementing radio control. The first step is to make all radio stations register. The second step is for the Ministry of Transportation to calibrate the sound waves of each radio station. The third step is to review the broadcasting content of each radio station. Now, the first and second steps have been completed, but the third step is still in preparation due to cumbersome procedures. The details are recorded as follows:

Circular on Registration 129

The first step in the Ministry of Transportation's plan for this matter is to order all commercial radio stations to register in order to start work later. Now all radio stations have complied, and even radio stations in the concession have gone to register. As for foreign radio stations, after the Ministry of Communication contacted them, they fully complied and were subject to the control of the Ministry of Communication as Chinese radio stations.

Calibration of Wave Numbers 130

Before registration, the broadcasting of each radio station was not very uniform, and some violated the international radio station regulations. According to international regulations, the radio station number used by our country is XG, while a small number of radio stations use XC. This number is used by Mexico, and our country cannot use it. There are also several foreign radio stations broadcasting numbers that are IUKO. This kind of game broadcasting is not applicable. Since registering with the Ministry of Transportation, the Ministry has ordered each radio station to disable this out-of-bounds number, and it has been completely banned.

Going to Inspection 131

The Ministry of Transportation also found that the messages sent by various radio stations often contain obscene songs and songs that obstruct public morals, giving citizens a bad impression. Radio was originally a tool for spreading culture. In this way, it is contrary to the principle. Therefore, it is planned to conduct inspections so that each radio station will submit the broadcast program to the Ministry for inspection in time before broadcasting. This will not only eliminate abuses, but also prevent the broadcasting time of each radio station from conflicting. This matter is currently being prepared, and it can probably be realized in a short period of time.

Arbitration of Labor Disputes over Wage Cuts in British-American Tobacco Factory 132

Xinsheng News Agency stated that the labor dispute over wage cuts in the British-American Tobacco Factory was previously guided by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Public Security Bureau. As a result, Labor No. 137 mediation records were made. The dispute over how many days of work per week after June 8th was resolved on the 5th of this month by the Social Affairs Bureau convening both labor and management to mediate. The labor representative requested that the number of days of work per week should not be less than four days in the future. The management representative agreed to work four days or more than four days per week from June 1st to July 10th. After July 10th, if it is necessary to work less than four days, the factory should first submit it to the bureau for approval, but it is only willing to be responsible for fulfilling this method and is unwilling to sign the mediation record. In addition, the labor representative requested that wages be paid as usual during the previous wage reduction period. The reason is that this has been the case in the past. The management representative believes that it was the management's generosity in the past. In the future, if you don't work, you will not be paid wages. After repeated persuasion by the chairman of the association, it failed to reconcile. The situation of the case dispute is serious and has been extended for more than a month. It was declared on the spot that the mediation was not established. The Social Affairs Bureau has now submitted a request to the Municipal Government to submit the case to arbitration in accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of the Labor Dispute Handling Law to eliminate disputes.

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that Shao Lizi, Chairman of Shaanxi Province, and Zhu Shaoliang, Chairman of Gansu Province, in order to revitalize the native tobacco industry in Shaanxi and Gansu, jointly telegraphed Song, the Minister of Finance, requesting approval to levy a special tax on native tobacco to benefit agriculture. The original telegram is as follows: Respected Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance, Nanjing. It has been observed that counties such as Gaolan in Gansu produce green, yellow, striped tobacco leaves, which are the only export products of Gansu. Merchants in Shaanxi have also been transporting and selling tobacco leaves here. In recent years, due to frequent disasters, the production volume has already sharply decreased. Furthermore, after the loss of the Northeast, the Niuzhuang and Dalian markets were cut off. Other regions have also been affected by the impact of imported cigarettes, and sales have been sluggish, leading to a crisis. Rural areas are declining, and markets are bleak. This is a major cause. Previously, I, Lizi, in order to support agriculture and revitalize local products, together with President Yu Youren, advocated improved production to facilitate sales. After I, Shaoliang, arrived in Gansu and examined the situation, I also felt that maintaining tobacco leaves was an essential measure to revive the local rural economy. We were just about to submit a request to the government when we learned that your ministry had implemented a special tax on native tobacco in seven provinces, including Jiangsu and Zhejiang, demonstrating your intent to protect local products and resist foreign goods. We deeply admire your grand plan. The situation in Shaanxi and Gansu is the same. Therefore, we are jointly telegraphing you to earnestly request that you consider the poverty of the Northwest and the scarcity of products, and include this type of native tobacco in the special tax zone along with the seven provinces for unified collection, so as to avoid the suffering of repeated taxation during transportation and sales. In this way, the markets and rural areas of Shaanxi and Gansu can prosper, and the national economy and the people's livelihood will benefit. We are sending this special telegram for your consideration and reply. Yours sincerely, Shao Lizi, Zhu Shaoliang, respectfully.

The Shanghai Cotton Cloth Association, in response to a letter from the Citizens' Association for Promoting National Products requesting strict sanctions against factories such as Gongzu, Zhou, etc., for privately importing enemy goods and reselling them with changed labels, sent a reply to the association yesterday, stating: Respectfully, we received your letter dated the 23rd of this month, stating that the Gongzu Sock Factory, Zhou Dingxin, Junchang, Tonghe Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Sanyang, Jiuyi, Yukang Cotton Weaving Factory, Yongyuan Mercerizing Factory, and Yixing Company,

illegally transported enemy yarn of the Dakang Yarn Factory's "Liuma" brand, changed it to the "Ren Zhong" brand of the Shenxin No. 5 Factory, and wove it into goods for sale in various ports. This not only deceives the public but also undermines the national product movement. You requested that we take strict measures to address this. Upon investigation, except for the Gongzu Sock Factory, the other factories are engaged in the silk and mercerized cotton weaving industry and are not within the scope of our association. Therefore, we have no way to handle this. However, to ensure that our members are aware and can distinguish between these products, we have already sent a notice as per your letter. We respectfully request your attention to this matter.

The Municipal Health Bureau is Constructing a Model Rural Health Area in Wusong 140

Building Treatment Facilities to Facilitate Villagers' Access to Medical Care

Instilling Health Knowledge to Improve Farmers' Health

The Municipal Health Bureau believes that health is of great importance to the revival of the rural economy. It is actively carrying out health facilities in the rural areas of the city. Recently, it has designated Wusong as a model rural health area in the city, allocated funds, and actively carried out construction. Although it is just beginning, it has achieved considerable results. The details are recorded below:

The Motivation for Constructing a Model Area 141

Before the January 28th Incident, the Municipal Health Bureau had already established a health office and a rural health model area office in Wusong. In terms of medical equipment, there were the Seaside Hospital and the Shanghai Medical College. However, due to the outbreak of the war, the hospital and school buildings were destroyed by artillery fire, causing all health administration to come to a standstill. After the ceasefire, the Health Bureau believed that the Wusong war zone had suffered severe damage and that it was necessary to actively restore various health facilities. At the same time, Tongji Medical College also requested the Municipal Government to cooperate, so that students of the Department of Public Health could practice here, and take this opportunity to penetrate into rural areas and strive for rural health movement. The Municipal Government approved this and decided that all construction expenses should be borne jointly by the Health Bureau and Tongji Medical College. The first phase of funding has been set at 40,000 yuan, and it was decided to carry out universal health education and health facilities movement in the Wusong area, and designate the area as a rural health model area, so that it can be promoted in the future.

Health Office to be Completed 142

After the January 28th Incident, all medical treatment facilities in the Wusong area were destroyed by artillery fire. Hundreds of thousands of farmers in Wusong felt the pain of having nowhere to seek medical treatment when they were sick. The Municipal Health Bureau, in view of this, once set up a mobile clinic car to travel to various villages and places where residents gather at any time, to facilitate medical treatment. However, due to the large number of people seeking medical treatment, it was difficult to cope with the situation. It was felt that it was necessary to establish a large-scale treatment center. The Health Bureau and Tongji Medical College jointly raised funds to build the Wusong Health District Office at the old site of the Seaside Hospital. The foundation stone was laid on July 1st, and it will be fully completed in the middle of next month. The interior will be equipped with various departments such as treatment. Before the official site is completed, a part of the Tongji Medical College's campus will be temporarily borrowed for office use, and public health expert Li Xuanguo will be hired as the director of the office, and technician Li Yuren, dispatched by the Health Bureau, will be the deputy director. The office will be the center, and the construction and publicity of rural health education will be gradually implemented. Although the work of the office is in its initial stage, it has achieved considerable results. In July, the number of people treated has been nearly a thousand. During the summer, significant achievements have also been made in various epidemic prevention works.

Implementing Rural Health Education 143

Revitalizing the countryside is the most important domestic policy measure in our country at present, and the revival of the rural economy is extremely important to the health problems of farmers. Without healthy farmers, everything in the countryside will not progress. The main purpose of the Health Bureau in constructing the Wusong Rural Health Model Area, in addition to diagnosing and treating diseases for farmers, its greatest task is to guide farmers to pay attention to health construction, and to take health education and improve farmers' health knowledge as the ultimate goal. It is heard that the initial implementation method will be carried out in three points: (1) Implement home visits for treatment, specially dispatching nurses and medical students to the homes of farmers with diseases to diagnose and treat them, and at any time convey health knowledge. (2) When patients come to the office for treatment, take the opportunity to provide instructions on health education and make them believe in the guiding agency. (3) Publicize openly, printing health propaganda materials, giving public health lectures, holding rural health movements, etc. In addition, carry out physical examinations, teach scientific methods, and eliminate pests, so that farmers in the area will become healthier day by day.

Guiding Factory Hygiene in the Area 144

There are many factories in the Wusong area. In addition to working hard in the countryside and schools, the office also pays attention to the hygiene equipment in the factories. Factory hygiene is more important than general hygiene. It is heard that the office is currently preparing everything and will start next month to conduct a thorough investigation of the hygiene conditions of each factory in the area, and send personnel to each factory at any time to provide guidance. If there are any improprieties, they will be corrected at any time to avoid various dangers and improve the health of workers.

The Truth About the Work Stoppage at the Wusong Machinery Factory on Both Railways 145

The Sand Casting Department has not yet resumed work

Dabai News Agency reports that workers at the Wusong Machinery Factory of the Two-Way Administration often have disputes over the work of the sand casting department. They have repeatedly requested the abolition of the contracting system. The union submitted a request to the Road Bureau for review in March of this year, but has not received a reply to date. At the beginning of August, the work of the sand casting department became light, and it was planned to implement a work reduction system to reduce the burden on the contractor, which aroused the attention of all the factory workers. Therefore, the association convened a joint meeting of group leaders and put forward a discussion. All agreed that if the contractor is not abolished one day, there will be a tendency to affect the entire factory in the future. Therefore, it was resolved to request the abolition of the contracting system within ten days, otherwise, all the workers in the factory would assist the workers in the department to make a corresponding response. The Wusong factory director and contractor Shan Rongsheng were notified immediately, and the trade union council was asked to forward the matter to the Road Bureau to abolish the system within a time limit. However, before ten days had passed and the turmoil in the sand casting department had not been resolved, the Road Bureau contracted the construction of dining cars and sleeper cars for the Pinghu through train to the carpenter department contractor Han Zepei. All the factory workers learned about this. The Road Bureau intends to restore the contracting system, and it is unknown what the intention is. The turmoil in the sand casting department has not yet been resolved, and now it is planned to try the contracting system in the carpenter department. The public was indignant and implemented a work stoppage on Monday morning (21st), and there were verbal conflicts and fights with each other. The union received the news and sent personnel to stop it, but two workers had been injured. In the afternoon of that day, the executive council of the union, fearing that the situation would escalate, specially sent the executive director Chen Bohua to investigate and stop it. However, the Road Bureau did not send personnel to the scene that day, so there was no result and the meeting was adjourned. The following morning (Tuesday), the work stoppage continued. At about 3 p.m., the bureau finally sent Yuan Boyang, together with party committee member Chen Chengshi, to persuade and accept the demands of the workers. The workers were satisfied and dispersed. The contracting system of the carpentry department has been abolished, so the workers have resumed work as usual. The Road Bureau has accepted the principle of abolishing the contracting system in the sand casting department, but it must wait for the workers in the department to state the reasons before reviewing it. Therefore, the work in the department has not yet resumed. Regarding this point, on the morning of the 23rd, more than 20 worker representatives, led by Party Committee member Chen Chengshi, contacted the Bureau, and then Chen Chengshi and important members of the factory's workers drafted a plan and then submitted it to the Road Bureau for adoption. However, since the work stoppage at the factory, the losses have been great, reaching 5,000 yuan per day. If it is not resolved quickly, the losses will be very large.

Third Hearing in the Box Corpse Case 147

Four Witnesses Summoned Yesterday for Detailed Questioning

At the End, the Portuguese Consul Suddenly Prohibited Public Attendance

丨The Final Hearing Will Be Held Today丨

Yesterday, the Portuguese Consulate summoned witnesses again in the box corpse case and opened the third hearing. At first, it was still open to the public, but later the presiding judge prohibited public attendance. The situation is recorded as follows:

Summoning Witnesses 148

The third preliminary hearing opened at 10 AM yesterday. The Portuguese Consul, Xiang Erfo, first brought the two main suspects, Padraile Ramidio and Zhou Shifu Ramidio, from the Xiamen Road Western Prison to the consulate for the third interrogation. Regarding the investigation of criminal evidence, there had been some progress after two hearings. Yesterday's third interrogation involved summoning four people to the case: Pi Dilai, a member of the Hongkou Fire Brigade, a dock worker named Zhang from the Huishan Wharf, Zhang He, the female landlord of No. 15 Jiaxing Road, and her son, Zhang Jingui. They were ordered to truthfully provide information to prove that the two main offenders committed the murder and moved the body.

Stating the Facts of the Case 149

When the Portuguese Consul General opened the court, he first asked the Portuguese Pidelai, who was a member of the fire brigade. Pi lived at No. 22 Jiaxing Road, which was opposite No. 15, where the murder took place. Pi Dilai testified that a Westerner first rented No. 15, and later he saw the Westerner arguing with a Chinese woman and hitting her. The Portuguese Consul immediately ordered Pi to identify the two defendants. Pi Dilai pointed out that Padraile was the person who committed the assault. The Portuguese Consul then asked if he had witnessed the assault. Pi said he did.

Identifying the Corpse Box 150

The Portuguese Consul then summoned the dock worker No. 7 from the Huishan Wharf to ask who delivered the iron box containing the corpse to the dock on August 5th, a Westerner or a Chinese person. The worker testified that it was a young man in Western clothes who delivered it, but he did not pay attention to their origin or appearance at the time, so he had forgotten. However, when the Portuguese Consul ordered him to identify the two defendants, the worker replied that it was difficult to identify them, but the box was definitely the correct one.

The Process of Moving the Corpse 151

Furthermore, the Portuguese Consul questioned the landlord Zhang He. Was the renter a foreigner? What was their name? Zhang He replied that it was a Westerner, but she did not know their name. While speaking, she pointed to Padraile and said that he was the one who rented the house. The Portuguese Consul asked if she knew his brother. She replied that she did not recognize him. He then asked who carried the iron box to the upstairs room. Zhang He said that two people carried it to the upstairs room at the same time. He then questioned her son, Zhang Jingui, who said that he had seen the landlord hitting a woman. At this point, the Portuguese Consul re-examined Pidelai's statement that the defendant's house was diagonally opposite his, and that the Chinese woman was indeed assaulted by Padraile Ramidio.

Prohibiting Public Attendance 152

At this point in the interrogation, the Portuguese Consul ordered all those attending the court and all news reporters to leave and changed the hearing to a secret trial of the witnesses and the two defendants. When the hearing opened yesterday, the lawyers hired by the defendants also attended the court to listen to the hearing and study the statements of the witnesses to defend the defendants. After the hearing was changed to a secret trial, it was not known what the results were.

Re-trial Tomorrow 153

The defendants and witnesses have been preliminarily tried three times, and the facts of the case have gradually become clear. It is now heard that the Portuguese Consulate has scheduled another joint trial of all nine witnesses in the case at the Consulate tomorrow, Saturday. This case in Shanghai will be concluded, and it will be decided to send it to Macau for trial in a formal court. The two defendants were returned to the Xiamen Road Western Prison at noon.

Police Investigation Not Yet Completed

Rescheduled for Re-Examination on the 31st

A Large Batch of Gold Bars Confiscated on the Haiyan Steamer 155

Since the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company sent police to inspect the Haiyun Steamer, a Wenzhou-bound vessel, a large number of illegally carried gold bars were found. The general situation is recorded below:

According to regulations, gold and silver ingots must be declared and taxed when brought into or out of the country. Entrusting a steamer to transport them and listing them on the manifest is in accordance with the procedures. However, a certain jewelry store in this port, recently in need of gold from Wenzhou colleagues, specially sent an employee with a large batch of gold to Wenzhou to distribute it to various colleagues' jewelry stores. At that time, they were greedy for small profits and did not declare it, nor did they hand it over to the shipping bureau. Instead, the employee carried it with them, boarded the steamer to Wenzhou, hoping to get through.

In order to prevent pirates from mixing in, the shipping companies have been sending police to inspect each departing steamer, which is very strict. The China Merchants Bureau specially sent eight Russian police officers, together with the wharf patrolmen, to inspect each steamer before departure, one hour before departure after all passengers had arrived. When the Haiyan Steamer was about to depart from Shanghai, the Russian police patrolmen also entered the cabin to search. In the official cabin, a large amount of gold was found. When the gold bars were confiscated, it was late at night, just before the Haiyan was about to depart. The Russian police patrolmen searched the official cabin and found a passenger's luggage with glittering gold, as many as thirty-four bars. The total weight, calculated at ten taels per bar, was also more than three hundred taels. Calculated at the market price, the value was tens of thousands of dollars. At that time, the inspectors, because they were privately carrying the gold in violation of the ban, immediately reported to the South Wharf to ask for instructions.

The South Wharf manager received the inspector's report and ordered the confiscated gold bars to be secretly sent to the South Wharf manager's office, and the person carrying the gold was also taken there. It was late at night, and there were not many people there. The witnesses were also taken to the manager's office. After repeated questioning by the manager, the passenger initially refused to tell the truth, only saying that they often went to Wenzhou to make jewelry for jewelry stores and were not privately transporting it. The gold bars were temporarily stored, and the name of the Shanghai jewelry store was asked. The South Wharf paid the way to inquire and confirmed the information, and then imposed a fine according to the regulations for illegally transporting goods. The confiscated gold bars were all returned. As for the amount of the fine, the parties kept it a secret, so it was impossible to know. The customs authorities have also received this news and have sent people to investigate the truth of the case.

Package of Lead Bars Passed Off as Fifty Dollars 156

Luckily the Shop Assistant Was Experienced, Otherwise, They Would Have Been Greatly Deceived

At precisely 3:45 PM the day before yesterday, two men, Huang Yu from Hubei and Wang Huanlian from Jiangxi, arrived together at the Yong Heng Gold Shop located at No. 210 Nanjing Road. They selected a gold bar and paid a deposit for it, weighing three taels and five mace, equivalent to 371 yuan at market price. Huang and Wang then took out 330 paper yuan and a package of cash, totaling 50 yuan, from their person. After the shop assistant, Fu Yulin, inspected it and found it correct, he turned to go upstairs to stamp the gold bar. Unexpectedly, Huang and Wang harbored ill intentions and took advantage of this time to replace the 50 yuan in cash with lead bars, shaping and wrapping them to resemble 50 yuan, hoping to deceive. However, when Fu came downstairs, he needed to return nine yuan in change, so he wanted to unwrap the package to take out the money. Huang and Wang, seeing that things were going wrong, hurriedly claimed to Fu that it was not necessary to make change at this time. The remaining nine yuan could be temporarily kept in the shop because they still needed to take the gold bar back home for his concubine to inspect. If she deemed it acceptable, they would return later. However, Fu refused and insisted on unwrapping the package to make the change. Seeing their plan foiled and in desperation, Huang and Wang had no choice but to turn and flee. Fu immediately blew the alarm whistle, and Chinese Constable No. 2835 and Chinese Detective Huang Yongji arrived, apprehending Huang Yuyi and Wang Huanlian. Together with the lead bars, paper money, and gold bar, they were taken to the Central Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, presented the case, stating that the police are now prosecuting them for attempted fraud under Article 363 of the Criminal Law. However, the case still needs to be investigated, so he requested a postponement. Fu Yulin, the shop assistant from Yong Feng Heng Gold Shop, also testified to everything. When questioned, the two defendants gave evasive answers. After the judge reviewed the statements, he ordered the two defendants to be remanded in custody, pending a further hearing in seven days after investigation.

His Wild Nature Doesn't Change and Always Causes Trouble

Municipal Police Bureau Re-establishes Police Training School 165

According to sources in the Municipal Police Bureau, the bureau has assigned [blank] Guangzeng and others to organize a committee to actively plan the re-establishment of the police training school. Progress has been made. The bureau has also allocated funds to the various district offices for construction. Details are listed below.

Training Police Officers 166

Before January 28th, the bureau had a police training school on Gongxing Road in Zhabei. However, it was shut down due to financial reasons. Recently, the bureau, recognizing the importance of training police officers, drafted a plan to re-establish the police training school and submitted it to the municipal government. After the municipal government approved it, the bureau assigned Commissioner Li Guangzeng and others to organize a committee. Various plans are now underway. However, part of the original site was destroyed by gunfire, and the remaining part is being used by the security team. Therefore, another solution is needed. The committee has located the old site of the Arsenal Factory. The premises are spacious with a large open area, making it very suitable for training police officers. They have submitted a request to the municipal government to forward to the Ministry of Military Affairs to borrow the site.

Repairing District Offices 167

Because the existing premises are insufficient, the bureau plans to move to the old Shanghai County Office, while the existing site will be sold at auction. The proceeds, estimated at over 100,000 yuan, will be allocated to repair the various district offices. Recently, the original site of the Fifth District Police Bureau in Zhabei was completely destroyed by gunfire. Although they are currently using rented premises, it is not suitable, and the rent is expensive. There is a public land east of the Zhabei Oriental Library, where the Jisheng Hospital was originally located. However, the hospital was also destroyed in the January 28th Incident. Therefore, the district plans to allocate this land to build a new district office. The plan has been submitted to the municipal government for approval.

Municipal Ferry's Cool-Off Night Service to be Discontinued 168

The intense heat of summer has subsided, and the weather is gradually turning cooler, especially in the mornings and evenings, like early autumn. The Municipal Ferry General Management Office's cool-off night service, which originally departed from the Bronze Man Pier at 8:30 PM every night, will be discontinued from August 28th.

Gaoqiao Public Bus Directly to the Beach 169

Service to begin on the 27th

Journey time less than 20 minutes

The Municipal Gaoqiao Public Bus used to run from Gaoqiao Pier to Gaoqiao Town. Passengers wishing to visit the beach or swim in the sea had to transfer to a small car or rickshaw, which was time-consuming and the roads were rough, causing inconvenience. Recognizing this, the Municipal Public Works Bureau, after consultation with the Public Works Bureau, opened the Gaoqiao-Beach Road, running directly from Gaoqiao Town to the beach. The entire road has been completed. From August 27th, the public bus will run directly from Gaoqiao Pier to the beach in less than 20 minutes. The ride is stable and fast, and the prices are affordable.

Residents of North Fujian Road Hold Anti-Rent Increase Meeting 171

The houses on the upper and lower banks of North Fujian Road, from the Old Zhabei Bridge to Tangjia Lane, are all leased by the Lao Gong Mao Foreign Firm. Recently, citing increased tap water and land taxes, they notified all residents that rents would be increased by 50% starting from July. The residents, due to the area being naturally quiet and the market extremely depressed after January 28th, which has not yet recovered, are finding it difficult to maintain the status quo. Economically, they cannot afford to bear the increased rent burden. They jointly requested assistance from the North Fujian Road Business Association, which has repeatedly contacted Lao Gong Mao but without result. Therefore, a majority of residents requested a meeting to discuss countermeasures. A meeting was convened for all residents of the road at 2:00 PM yesterday (August 24th) to discuss the measures. 92 representatives attended, and He Xiangsheng, Liu Xuemei, and Yuan Bingqi were elected as the presidium. First, the chair reported on the process. Then, the residents expressed their opinions. In general, they were all unwilling to increase the rent, and some even pointed out that in other more prosperous areas, there were examples of requesting rent reductions, and they also wanted to express their desire for rent reductions. The atmosphere was very tense. Finally, countermeasures were agreed upon as follows: (1) The market is depressed and difficult to maintain. A reluctant increase of 5% to maintain the relationship between the landlord and the residents. (2) Each resident should first prepare funds to oppose the rent increase and deposit them in the bank. (3) He Xiangsheng, Bao Jiebei, and Chen Baode were elected as members of the residents' reserve fund management committee. (4) Organize the North Fujian Road Residents' Anti-Rent Increase Committee. (5) The reserve fund will be collected immediately after the procedures are completed.

Newly Invented Chinese Typewriter

Seeking Capitalist Cooperation 173

The Chinese typewriter, patented by the Ministry of Industry of the National Government, has been successfully developed and marketed since 1930 by Mr. Yu Binqi, a mechanical engineering technician who returned from studying in Japan. Certain foreign products have disappeared from the market, and the machine has been improved repeatedly. All raw materials are entirely domestically produced. The machine is sensitive, the characters are steel, strong and durable, and will not be damaged for ten years. Hundreds of units have been purchased by government agencies at all levels, banks, companies, commercial firms, and foreign firms across the country, and all have praised it. Because the inventor lacks capital, the supply cannot meet demand, and there is no formal factory, resulting in high costs, hindering the popularization of culture, which is a great regret. Moreover, there is an order from the National Government that all agencies should pay attention to the Chinese language in the future, and business will certainly develop more. It is definitely not a small-scale operation that one person can control the progress of culture. He is now willing to cooperate with Chinese nationals who can raise 10,000 to 20,000 yuan in capital, or sell the invention rights. However, it is limited to Chinese nationals. Those who are interested in this business can write to Mr. Ma Chonggan of this newspaper, who will arrange a face-to-face meeting to discuss everything.

Freedom of Marriage Denied, Woman Mourns Her Fate and Commits Suicide 174

Hong Liangcheng, 48 years old from Anhui, currently residing in Beiping, works in military and political circles. Three months ago, when Japanese troops attempted to invade Tianjin, he brought his family to Shanghai to take refuge, residing at No. 7 Chongfu Lane, Route Foch in the French Concession. His sixth younger sister, Hong Lin, also known as Xiaomei, 27 years old, graduated from a certain school, is knowledgeable, and unmarried. With her parents deceased, her marriage is arranged by her elder brother and sister-in-law. Her brother intends to marry Lin to a northerner, but Lin objects and plans to find a suitable match in the south. On the second day of this lunar month, it was Liangcheng's birthday, and all his sisters came to wish him a happy birthday. During the dinner, they discussed Lin's marriage, causing an argument between the siblings. Lin, thinking of her deceased parents and denial of freedom of marriage, contemplated suicide. On the evening of the 23rd, she secretly swallowed raw opium. At midnight, her sister-in-law discovered her and tried to save her by giving her soapy water, but it was ineffective. She was taken to Paulun Hospital by car at 3:00 AM yesterday morning, but the treatment was ineffective. She died at 6:00 AM. The hospital reported to the Xinzha Police Station, which informed the French Police, who sent detectives to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home to examine the body. They also investigated the circumstances of the suicide. At noon that day, they reported to the Second Special District Court. The local prosecutor went to the site and determined that the deceased, Hong Lin, had committed suicide by taking poison. The official ordered her brother, Hong Liangcheng, to prepare a coffin for burial.

A Woman Commits Suicide in a Room in Grief After Childbirth 175

Zhu Zhaochao, a laborer from Gaoyou, 37 years old, residing at No. 13 Xiangyan Bridge in Hongkou, married Zhu Zhushi, 38 years old, 19 years ago. They had four sons, but all died prematurely. The woman was saddened and resentful, developing a chronic illness that could not be cured. She felt her life was miserable and not worth living, so she committed suicide by hanging herself in the room the night before last. When her husband woke up and saw his wife hanging, he was shocked and tried to save her, but it was too late. He mourned loudly over her body and reported to the Third Precinct of the Fifth District, ordering the local guarantor, Xu Jinlin, to report to the local court for an autopsy. Zhu also went to the court to request that the autopsy be waived.

Police Use Force, Causing Negotiations 178

Yesterday at around 11:00 AM, a conflict occurred between the owner of the Yiqingyong Wine Shop, Shu Yuanhe, at No. 76 [blank] Lu, Nanyang Bridge, French Concession, and armed police. The police used force, and a Chinese constable from the French Police was injured while trying to stop them. As a result, the shop owner, Shu Yuanhe, was arrested by the police. Afterwards, the police were notified, and the Wine Merchants Association investigated and negotiated. The investigated details are as follows:

Strict Inspection of Tax Evasion 179

Yesterday morning, Shu Yuanhe, the owner of Yiqingyong at No. 76 [blank] Lu, Nanyang Bridge, and an old clerk were transporting over ten loads of wine when they were inspected by patrol police from the Second District in the Chinese Concession. The police believed they were evading stamp tax and took Shu and the wine to the district office. Shu stated that the wine tax had been changed to the Tobacco and Alcohol Special Tax and the Domestic Wine Fixed Tax on July 1st, and stamp tax had long been abolished. He also had a letter from the Wine Merchants Association to prove it. At around 10:00 AM, he was released.

Police Use Force 180

At around 11 o'clock, two armed police officers and three or four plainclothes officers went to the shop to demand one yuan in overdue liquor charges. The shop owner, Shu Yuanhe, pleaded with them, saying that they didn't need to repay the one yuan debt and only needed to refrain from detaining tax-bearing alcohol. A conflict arose from their verbal exchange, leading to the use of force and a brawl. The liquor jars and vats were destroyed. Upon seeing this, the shop assistants blew a whistle, and French constables arrived to stop them, but to no avail. The police officers drew their bayonets and stabbed Yuanhe fiercely. Two Chinese constables also suffered cuts on the back of their hands. As a result, the shop owner was arrested and taken to the Second District Headquarters.

Lost Collar Tab 181

The two Chinese constables failed to stop them and returned to the police station to report. The head constable immediately dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to the scene. The police officers had already left, but a police collar tab with the number 1154 was found on the ground, along with two broken liquor jars and seven vats. The ground was covered in spilled liquor. The shop owner's son, Changjin, immediately asked a photographer, Mr. Liu, to take photos as evidence for future negotiations. He also went to the French police station to report all the details of the incident.

Ongoing Negotiations 182

After receiving the report, the political department of the French police station dispatched Inspector Cheng Ziqing to the Second District Headquarters first and then to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for negotiations. After receiving the report, the liquor industry association immediately reported the details to the Special Tax Bureau for Tobacco and Alcohol, requesting swift negotiations with the Municipal Public Security Bureau.

Completion of the Jinhua River Railway Bridge on the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway 185

Jinhua Dispatch: The newly built Jinhua River Railway Bridge on the Jinyu section of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, located approximately eight li west of Jinhua County, spans the Jinhua River. The bridge consists of twelve arches and is over 900 feet long. The bridge piers are constructed of reinforced concrete, and the bridge beams and deck are made of steel, with a total weight of approximately 7,500 tons. The steel plate bridge deck project was contracted to the Shanghai Yangzi Construction Company. The materials were ordered from a renowned German factory. It is said that the materials were delayed by a month after leaving the German factory and faced logistical challenges in transporting them from the Shanghai factory to the construction site, resulting in a slight delay in the commencement of work. Fortunately, the company accelerated the construction, and the project was completed on the 22nd of this month. The installation of the bridge beams, from the initial placement to the complete completion, took only two months, and the erection of the third to tenth arches was completed in just one month. The speed and efficiency with which this challenging project was completed in such a short period are truly admirable.

Rickshaw Guild Hosts Banquet for the Press Yesterday 186

Reporting on the Inspection of Vehicles by the Concession Authorities

Gu Songmao, Zhu Heqing, and others from the Shanghai Rickshaw Guild hosted a banquet for newspaper reporters at Xinghua Lou last night at 7 p.m. to report on the inspection of vehicles by the concession authorities. According to them, the rickshaws operating in Shanghai, particularly those in the Public Concession, have always been the best. Since the January 28th Incident, vehicles have been unable to be inspected, resulting in a small number of unclean vehicles operating. The Public Concession authorities have rigorously rectified this, instructing vehicle owners to have their vehicles inspected monthly. However, since May, the industry has effectively cleaned and improved vehicles. They have been approved by the Public Works Department to employ inspectors for regular inspections and guidance. This will encourage rickshaw pullers to maintain their vehicles and keep them clean, avoiding the need for monthly inspections. The Public Works Department has agreed to withdraw the monthly inspection order. As for the former owner of the Flying Yesterday Company, due to their disinclination to operate the business in 1928, they sold all vehicles, factory buildings, etc., to Gu Jun Songmao and others. This was a complete sale, without any gifts or bequests to others. The newspaper report was a misunderstanding.

Publishing a Commemorative Album

The Nanjing Global News Agency, founded a year ago by Li Gongpu and Jin Keqian, is dedicated to translating and compiling opinions from abroad and domestic sources, issuing domestic news dispatches, and translating domestic political and economic news into English, French, and other languages for distribution to foreign opinion outlets and cultural, peace, and religious organizations. Letters 191

I have checked your newspaper today. The local news column on the fourth page states that the two warships were converted into merchant ships, and that Zhou Houkun, the chief of the shipping section, went to Beijing to inspect Jing'an, etc. This is indeed a misinterpretation. I have not been to Beijing in the past two months, and I have never inspected Jing'an. Please publish it in the letters column to correct it. Sincerely, Zhou Houkun, August 24.

Dear Editor, I have just read your newspaper's report on the 23rd of this month, on the fourth page, about the police chief of the second precinct's inner service being bribed to release the head of the smugglers of small goods, Yu Maogui, and being replaced by A Da (nickname Xiao Mapi) and three others. It is said that I am also suspected of a major crime, which is very shocking. After investigating the case, a total of six people, including Yu Maogui, were arrested. When the case was handed over, Yu Maogui happened to have a fever, so he asked his friend Zhang Shaorong to ask the police chief to temporarily keep Yu Maogui for medical treatment on the way and send his nephew Yu Ada to the case instead. However, I was not aware of the previous situation beforehand, and the police chief did not report it. After learning the information, I immediately investigated and sent the police to arrest Yu Maogui and the guarantor Zhang Shaorong. Together with the police chief of the inner service, they were all sent to the bureau for interrogation. I have no suspicion of involvement in this case. Now, what is reported in your newspaper is not consistent with the facts. I should write a letter and hope to check it and give a correction to clear up the doubts. Sincerely, Jiang Sheng, Chief of the Second Precinct of the Third District, August 24.

Dear Editor, I have just read a news item on the fourth page of your newspaper on August 24 about investigating the illegal detention of people, which is not consistent with the facts. I am especially writing a special letter to clarify and correct it, so as to fulfill the responsibility of the local notary. I hope that you will immediately publish it in the correction column to correct the hearing. Please, Shenbao Museum, Jin Maoji Xieji Transportation Company, Nanzhan Tonghe Xie Company, and Tongshang Xingji Company. August 24.

Financial News from the UK and the US 192

Reuters, London, 24th: Today, the price of silver has shrunk. The near term is 17 pence 875, and the far term is 18 pence. Both the near and far terms are down 0.0625 from yesterday's price.

At 3 p.m. today, the London to New York exchange rate was as follows: One pound sterling equals four dollars and fifty-one cents. One dollar equals four shillings and four pence and seven hundred forty-eight.

New York, 24th: Today, the opening price of silver in this market for the long term is longer than yesterday's closing price by 0 to 8 pounds. However, the price in May shrunk by 18 pounds.

Weather Report 193

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday stated that the weather will be cloudy or overcast, with localized thunderstorms in the north. There will be south winds south of the Yangzhou River Estuary, and winds will be undirected in other areas. In addition, within the 24 hours before 3 pm yesterday, the temperature in this city was a high of 95.5 and a low of 74.7. On the same day last year, the high was 88.7 and the low was 73.0.

Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society 194

Opened in Qingdao Yesterday

(Qingdao, 24th) The 10th annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society opened at 9 am on the 24th. More than 200 members and guests attended. Ma Yinchu, the chairman, delivered the opening speech. Ministry of Education Orders Departments and Bureaus to Report on Education Expenses Within a Deadline 195

(Nanjing, 24th) The Ministry of Education telegraphed to various departments and bureaus on the 24th, stating that the 22nd year has already begun, and all matters concerning the investigation and statistics of social education expenses within this year should be continued. Two types of forms have been prepared and sent by telegram. One is to investigate provincial social education expenses and report them within three days of the arrival of the telegram, and the other is to investigate local social education expenses in various counties and cities and report them within two months of the arrival of the telegram. Please follow the instructions and do not delay.

The curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools that were previously drafted by the Curriculum Standards Drafting Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools organized by the Ministry of Education have been successively announced by the Ministry of Education. It is reported that the Ministry of Education will soon begin to organize a committee to draft curriculum standards for normal schools. After domestic normal education experts are hired separately, they will immediately engage in drafting work.

China Library Association Assigns Qiu Kaiming to Attend the International Library Conference (2) 199

Investigation Undertakings

(1) National Library Investigation: The national library survey form compiled and printed by the association has always been valued by the academic community. The one printed last year was the fourth revised edition. At the same time, the Department of Social Education of the Ministry of Education also printed a book of national library survey forms, which was co-authored with the Public Education Museum, so the number was relatively small. However, among them, the provincial, municipal, and county libraries have many places where the original form of the association can be corrected. Now, the association has continued to investigate for a year and has continued to increase. It plans to re-edit and record the expenses, the number of books in the collection, the classification and cataloging methods, and the reading status of each newspaper to form a systematic survey form, which will be published in a special issue in the 9th volume of the society newspaper, and will also be printed separately for purchase and reference. (2) Provincial Library Investigation: Last year, Hebei and Sichuan provinces sent members to investigate on behalf of the association. In addition to the reports from Hebei Province being published successively in the 7th volume of the society newspaper and the 2nd issue of the 6th volume of the quarterly magazine, the report on the investigation of Sichuan Province Library was published in the 3rd issue of the 8th volume of the society newspaper published this year because it was sent later. This year, in order to improve the guiding principles of library education and promote the development of library services, Shen Zurong, the president of the Wu Xiang Wenhua Library School, was specially entrusted to investigate the libraries along the way from Hubei to Pingdi via Jiangxi, Anhui, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang provinces.

President Chi went north from Han in early April for a period of one month before completing the task (3) Periodical Investigation: The publication of periodicals in our country is becoming more and more frequent, and there is a lack of complete catalogs, so the subscription of periodicals is the most difficult thing for libraries. Since the 16th year of the Republic of China, the Association has had periodical survey catalogs published in the association newspaper every period, which can be used for libraries to refer to. After the 20th year of the Republic of China, the number of new publications in the past two years has become more prosperous, and experts Li Wenyi have continued to compile the list, which will be published in the 9th volume of the association newspaper in the future (4) Bookstore Investigation: The association has always been very committed to the investigation of bookstores in various places, but our country has a vast territory, and it is difficult for the association to send people to investigate one by one, so it must rely on the support of libraries in various places to be able to help. This year, members were again entrusted to investigate, and the returned items were very clear, especially the Guangxi Statistical Bureau Library provided the most assistance (5) Rare Book Investigation: The Rare Book Investigation Committee was initially presided over by Liu Yizheng, and the achievements over the years have been considerable. This year, the special committee was reorganized, and the rare book investigation was merged into the Board Investigation Committee, which was still presided over by Liu. The following Song and Yuan editions will be investigated one by one: (1) Jiaye Library, (2) Songjiang Han's Library, (3) Nanhai Kang's Library,

Classification and Cataloging

The Classification Committee has made great progress since collecting the current classification methods. After the Jiangsu Provincial Guoxue Library's Cataloging and Classification Outline was published, the Association published it in the 5th issue of the 8th volume of the Society's newspaper. The classification is detailed, and the outline is in the outline, which can be used as a reference for those who are engaged in classification in various libraries. The society has also published Bi Xiaopo's Modern Library Cataloging Method in the 8th volume, which has been printed and will be published in a separate edition. As for reference books on cataloging, such as Ming and Qing Books Collected by , Ye Qidong's Examination of the Four Libraries' Complete Book Catalog Edition, and Xing Yunlin's Research on the Details of the Book Style Catalog, are all the results of the members' efforts in recent years. After the reorganization of the Cataloging Committee, Qiu Kaiming, the chairman of the Cataloging Committee, formulated a national library cataloging survey form, and first engaged in investigating the cataloging status of various libraries as preparation for improving cataloging methods and standardizing cataloging regulations. The form has been sent to each library, and a small number have not been completed, so the statistics cannot be published.

Jinan University's Overseas Chinese Student Examinations Held Yesterday and Today 207

Dutch Overseas Chinese Merchants Personally Send Their Children to Take the Exam

National Jinan University's recruitment of new overseas Chinese students this year has seen enthusiastic returns to the country to take the exam. This has been previously reported. It is learned that yesterday (the 24th) and today are the dates for the overseas Chinese student examinations for the middle school department. The number of applicants yesterday reached over two hundred and ten. Examinations for Chinese and English were held in the morning, and tests were conducted in the afternoon. Today, examinations for mathematics and history and geography will be held in the morning, and Japanese tests and physical examinations will be conducted in the afternoon. According to reports, the average performance in the subjects tested yesterday was good, indicating the progress of overseas Chinese education over the years and not being inferior to that of various regions in the country. Considering that overseas Chinese students are new to the country and unfamiliar with the environment, with various inconveniences in terms of habits and language, the school provides special treatment. Those who notified the school of their arrival date in Shanghai were met at the port and allowed to stay on campus in advance. The student self-government association of the school also organized a candidate guidance office to assist the school authorities in providing practical guidance. Many of the overseas Chinese students who were staying with relatives and friends off campus were accompanied by their relatives and friends to take the exam yesterday. Liu Jintang, a leader of overseas Chinese merchants in the Dutch East Indies (currently the director of the Chinese Association in Bandung, the principal of the Bandung Zhongping School, etc.), personally sent his children back to China to take the exam this time. He visited the school in detail yesterday and was greatly impressed. Furthermore, the second round of examinations for overseas Chinese students in the university department is scheduled for the 28th and 29th of this month. Over a hundred people have already prepared to take the exam.

Edited by Ms. Xu Yuwen

Diary of the British Wimbledon World Tennis Championships (5) 229

Special Correspondence from London by Yizhi

July 3rd (Monday)

(No games were held on Sunday, July 2nd) Today, a tranquil atmosphere pervades every part of the grounds. The overflowing crowds from Saturday are nowhere to be seen, and neither are the royal and noble spectators. No unexpected events occur in the matches. The weather remains consistently sunny, and even the weather forecast office expresses optimism. It has been nine days without rain, and today marks the tenth. Today is the start of the second week. The weather is exceptionally hot; the London thermometer rises to 84 degrees. It is even hotter during the day. Both those in the stands and those leaving the grounds are sweating profusely, seeking the comfort of the shade. The Wimbledon grass courts, parched by the prolonged drought, desperately need rain. Standing on them, one feels secure and not at all slippery. On the center court, Crawford's victory over Hughes was like a raging torrent sweeping him away. Hughes no longer exhibited the bravery he displayed when defeating Sydes the previous day; he was merely like clay in the hands of a potter. Crawford, on the other hand, was precise, confident, relaxed, and agile, possessing an admirable command of the game. He demonstrated his improved tennis skills with forceful smashes executed with unwavering precision. In the first two sets, he won five consecutive games and conceded only one. In the third set, Hughes gradually regained his composure, taking a 4-2 lead. However, the Australian ultimately prevailed with a score of 7-5. Crawford's victory was expected, but not by such a wide margin.

Stoffen, appearing half-crippled from fatigue, deserves commendation for winning the first set against Cochon, and for fighting fiercely in the second set. Stoffen was hampered by his injury, his injured finger causing considerable inconvenience. Ultimately, he lost due to his cautious play. Stoffen pressured Cochon with his powerful serves, but his mistake was to follow up his serves to the net instead of waiting behind the baseline for weaker returns. Cochon seemed flustered, lacking energy and power. He gradually recovered his form and committed numerous errors, which was surprising given his recent performances. His upcoming match against Vines will be a major test. In the fourth set, Stoffen only managed to win one game.

The leading British female player, Miss Hee (right), is defeated by Mrs. Marty (left).

Morell and Vines engaged in a fierce four-set battle, mostly along the baseline, alternating between sharp cross-court shots and aggressive volleys at the net. The match was held on center court. Morell won the third set 6-3, but did not appear to be a likely winner overall. The match proceeded quietly. Vines gave the impression of not exerting his full effort, constantly changing his shots as if experimenting with various techniques. Sometimes she let the ball go where it may, as if only wanting to hit it cleanly. She would tighten and loosen her grip, making it difficult for her opponent to predict her next move.

Vines won the first set 6-1, demonstrating how tennis should be played. Morell was not as weak as the score suggested. Morell's footwork was hindered by her jumping, which disrupted her serve. After breaking Morell's serve to take a 4-1 lead, Vines reached her peak but then stopped using her fastest shots, giving Morell no chance to respond.

Vines played more gently in the second set. After a 4-4 tie, she broke Morell's serve and then won her own. Vines seemed to be putting on a show. She conceded the third set and then accelerated again in the fourth, taking a 4-1 lead and winning 6-3. Vines appeared thoughtful during the match, but her spirit was excellent. Once, after winning a point by hitting Morell's serve, she insisted on a replay because she had touched the ball with her racquet. Morell seemed more susceptible to the heat than Vines, and admired Vines' victory. She occasionally exclaimed beautiful sounds before the ball arrived. A year ago, on a court that was less dry and firm than today, Austin defeated Sato. Today, however, things were very different. After losing the first two sets, Austin was unable to recover. Austin broke Sato's serve in the first set, offering a glimmer of hope, but Sato responded with pressure to seize the set 7-5. Sato gained an early advantage in the second set, intensifying his pace to win 6-3. Sato, satisfied with his easy victory, eased up, and Austin won the third set 6-2 with careful and powerful shots. Such caution often leads to failure, and ultimately, Austin's serve secured the fourth set. Notably, the shots controlling the game were not deep, and there was little footwork.

With the match tied, the aroused Sato began to pressure the struggling Austin, taking a 4-2 lead. He served powerfully to make it 5-2. In the final point of the deciding game, Austin exerted all his strength. There were two deuces, and Sato finally won 6-2 with a powerful shot.

The match lacked excitement and intensity, but it was a steady, attentive, and thoughtful contest. Sato, unlike Austin, had more stamina to recover in the fourth set, and he was able to apply pressure early in the fifth set. The center court was filled with spectators, all hoping for an English victory, but they were in good spirits and gave Sato a full round of applause.

Mrs. Bayot won 6-4, 6-1. The Swiss woman gained momentum and won three consecutive games, causing some surprise. However, Mrs. Marty seemed impatient in the hot weather and allowed her to dictate the game, making some unnecessary mistakes. In the second set, Bayot ran out of strength and surrendered without resistance.

Spears and Burke, against the veteran team of Boughlot and Bruin, tied the second set 6-2, raising hopes for a comeback. Ball's sweeping shots mixed with inexplicable errors, and Bruin's overhead smashes lacked accuracy. With Spears' serves frequently winning points and Burke providing solid support, there seemed to be a chance of continued success. However, they gradually succumbed to errors, especially Spears. The French seized the opportunity to win with two scores of 6-4.

On the outer court, Mrs. Godfrey and Mrs. Mykal defeated Miss Skrivan and Miss Siga 7-5, 7-5 in a special match. More investigation is needed in doubles matches. Her posture was not good, and Siga lacked a significant amount of strength. Gomi's victory was well-deserved. Mixed doubles matches are underway, but nothing noteworthy has occurred.

Spring and Autumn

The Mystery of Legs 230

— Zhan Lu

Everyone has legs, but the way they are used varies. I think: a policeman's legs are made of telephone poles; a postman's legs are made of bamboo from the garden; a rickshaw puller's legs are made of drumsticks; a wealthy tycoon's legs are made of coffin planks. These four constitute the mystery of legs.

The first mystery is easy to guess. When a policeman stands guard, his legs remain firmly planted, almost like a telephone pole, so they are said to be made of telephone poles.

The second mystery is that a postman's legs and bamboo from the garden certainly have some similarities. Bamboo brings news of peace, and a postman's legs also carry the mission of delivering news of peace. This is a similarity in nature. Bamboo is wrapped in green bamboo skin, and a postman's legs are also wrapped in green gaiters. This is a similarity in form.

The third mystery is that when a rickshaw puller runs, his feet hit his buttocks. Although they don't actually hit his buttocks, they are very close. Since his buttocks become a drum, his legs become drumsticks, so they are said to be made of drumsticks.

The fourth mystery is that wealthy tycoons rarely use their legs. They sit at home and want something, they don't need to move their honorable legs. They just press the electric bell, and if they want tea, it's tea; if they want wine, it's wine; if a concubine comes, the servants also come. When they go out, their legs are always inside a car, so there's even less need to walk. These two rarely used honorable legs can be labeled with two red paper slogans. What words should the slogans use? You can imitate the words pasted on coffin planks and call them: "Prepared but not used."

Yellow, White, Black 231

— Xianxian

White people are the darlings of heaven, the rulers of this world. Black people are specially created by God to be slaves to white people. Generation after generation, they are always ruled by white people. No one can blame anyone for this; the only blame lies in the differences in skin color.

Besides white and black people, there are also us yellow people, who are neither white nor black, stuck in the middle. It's truly awkward.

In the past, fashionable men and women, seeing white people being so incredibly white, wanted to artificially transform their yellow skin, which they were born with, into white, pretending to be white people from the ruling class. They would apply half a pound of vanishing cream and a thick layer of face powder to their face and hands every day, looking like Cao Mengde from the opera stage. But no matter how much you dress up, even if you paint a layer of white paint on your face, you're still a yellow person and can't pretend to be white. Although this is very regrettable, this is how God created things. Cows eat rice stalks, ducks eat grain, and no one can envy anyone.

Recently, fashionable men and women have transformed into modern men and women. They have also changed their style of dyeing their skin and are competing to become black. Their skin, which was originally sallow, has gradually become one percent whiter after years of pickling in vanishing cream and powder. Now, suddenly, large numbers of people are rushing to the Takahashi beach, soaking in the seawater, lying on the sand, and letting the sunlight, at about 100 degrees, bake their unsightly yellow skin from yellow to brown to black, so black that Indians shy away and Negroes concede defeat. Only then is it considered beautifully black.

It was still understandable to want to be a white person with a yellow base in the past, because they wanted to jump from the quasi-slave status of a semi-colony to a ruler. After decades of drawing a tiger, they achieved nothing. Now they suddenly want to become black people with a yellow base. I really don't know what they're thinking. Could it be that being a quasi-slave isn't crisp enough, so they want to take a step further and seek to be a formal slave of white people?

I don't think a black person with a yellow base is more popular than a formal black person. We should still follow Korea and Manchuria and be slaves to yellow people.

A Visit to the Women's Temperance Home Economics School 232

— Fang Zhicheng

In recent months, I have often heard news about the Women's Temperance Home Economics School. This not only piqued my curiosity, but I also needed to find such a school to remedy my daughter's lack of education. However, to be cautious, I first went to visit. The school is located at the intersection of Jiangwan and Xiangyin Roads. That day, I walked into the school gate, handed in my business card, and after a while, a simply dressed middle-aged woman came out. She nodded amiably to me, and I explained my intention. She said, "We welcome your visit to our school. Please come in!" As she spoke, she pointed her hand forward. I followed her up the stone steps and into the building. To the right was a very clean reception room, and it is said that the tablecloths on the tables were all woven by the students themselves. Behind the reception room was a staircase. To the left was a classroom. The teacher was teaching a lesson, teaching new methods of infant care. Behind it was a large classroom where more than thirty students were preparing for a microbiology lesson. I stood there, and they didn't mind at all. Later, we went up to the second floor, where there were six rooms of various sizes, one was an infant care practice room, one was a practical kindergarten, and the rest were classrooms, sewing, and embroidery rooms. The third floor was the teachers' dormitory. Walking back, we arrived at the kitchen and dining hall. At that time, there were several girls in white aprons cooking in the kitchen. After being introduced by the female teacher, I said, "Your aprons are so elegant!" They were not shy at all, and one of them said, "This is our self-made uniform." The receptionist smiled at me and said, "We don't normally allow men to visit, but since your daughter is coming to study, we'll make an exception!" I thanked her a few times, and we went to the simple but very clean bedrooms. As I was about to leave, she told me again: "Our school was founded by the Women's Christian Temperance Union. The purpose is: 1) to cultivate healthy motherhood, 2) to train hard-working women to engage in rural women's liberation movements in the future or to work as managers in urban families; 3) to create opportunities for girls from poor families to study and to remedy the lack of education for a group of women who have dropped out of school." I think this school is well-run and has excellent content, so I am introducing it to readers and offering it to women who aspire to study home economics. (Remuneration declined)

Taking a Noon Nap 233

— Xia Tianwu

"Noon nap," is commonly referred to as "taking a midday siesta." Indeed, during the long summer days, the days are short and the nights are long. People are busy all day, and at night, they still can't get a good sleep. For example, poor people are enemies with mosquitoes and bedbugs, hunting them all night; the middle class can't afford electric fans and air conditioning, suffering from the oppressive heat and fanning themselves incessantly, unable to sleep soundly until dawn; the wealthy live in a world of leisure at night, with dance halls, movie theaters, and grand hotels...

Therefore, in summer, people from all three classes, upper, middle, and lower, do not get enough sleep at night.

Lack of sleep at night makes people feel tired during the day, especially with the midday heat and the quieter streets. After a satisfying meal, they sit quietly in a corner. "Reading already feels heavy on the brow, and lying down brings comfort to the bones." If the eyelids naturally droop, then having time for a "midday siesta" is a rare blessing.

Here are two poems that perfectly express the sweetness of "taking a midday siesta":

"Waiting for the futon, the sleep is long, the host and guest forget each other. Soon the guest leaves and the host wakes, half the west window has no sunset." -- Lu Fangweng.

"Paper screen, tile pillow, bamboo mat, a book tossed aside, a long midday dream. Waking up with a chuckle and a smile, several fishing flutes sound in the waves." -- Cai Chizheng.

Schools have summer vacations because students "doze off" in class. Otherwise, if classes were held as usual during the summer vacation, two-thirds of the time would be spent "dozing off." If people are fortunate enough to take a "midday siesta" every day in summer, it shouldn't be considered laziness, because it is a physiological function. Ma Xiangbo once said: "My way of maintaining health is not some miraculous method. I eat and drink in moderation every day, and after lunch, I close my eyes and sit quietly, eliminating distracting thoughts, and take a nap..." This shows that "taking a midday siesta" is still a secret to good health. It may seem uneconomical to waste time on a "midday siesta" every day, but overall, extending one's lifespan compensates for the time spent each day. Therefore, "taking a midday siesta" is an economical and life-extending method.

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 234

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 14: Difficult Marriage, Hesitant Worries; Inviting Friends for a Small Gathering, Reluctantly Recalling the Past

Mrs. Jiang stood up, wiping her wet hands with her apron, and repeatedly said, "Please come in and sit, please come in and sit." Guan Yaowu entered the house, took off his hat, and bowed deeply to Mrs. Jiang, saying, "Congratulations, congratulations!" Mrs. Jiang smiled, "What's there to congratulate?" Guan Yaowu said, "Is my cousin at home?" Mrs. Jiang said, "You are an elder brother. If you intend to make this a good match with my cousin, you have to do it properly and don't joke with her. Please sit down." Mrs. Jiang threw out the laundry water, swept the house hastily, and then sat down opposite Guan Yaowu. Immediately she stood up again and smiled, "Look at me, I'm so busy that I forgot to prepare tea and cigarettes for the guest." Guan Yaowu waved his hand, "Don't bother, I didn't come for tea and cigarettes. I'm now asking you a question as a cousin. You always approve of this marriage and have no objections?" Mrs. Jiang said, "Even in business, you can't go back and forth. Marriage is a big deal. There's no reason to say one thing today and another thing tomorrow. But there are still many things to discuss. First..." Before she could state her condition, she heard a crisp voice from inside the house calling "Mom." Mrs. Jiang thought that maybe her daughter had some preconditions, so she answered and went into the room. She saw Guizhi sitting in the room alone, looking up at the ceiling, smiling slightly, just calling "You come in." Mrs. Jiang said, "There's nothing wrong. Why did you call me in?" Guizhi said, "If there was something, I wouldn't dare to ask you to come in. Didn't you say yesterday that you wouldn't care anymore? Since you're not caring anymore, why are you babbling so much in the outer room?" Guan Yaowu said, "Cousin, what's wrong with you? Is there anything else to discuss?"
